</style><style name="respview.client.js" mode="after" wrap="ready">
  /* Only run screener card JS if screener elements exist on this page */
  if(!document.getElementById('card-intro')){ return; }

  var defined = function(s,c){ return (c||document).querySelector(s); };
  var definedAll = function(s,c){ return [].slice.call((c||document).querySelectorAll(s)); };

  var CARDS = ['card-intro','card-qs1','card-qzip','card-qage','card-qgender','card-qvote24','card-party'];
  var cur = 0;
  var total = CARDS.length - 1;

  /* ---- find Decipher question element by label ---- */
  function findQ(q){
    return document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]')
        || document.querySelector('.question input[name*="'+q+'"]');
  }
  /* auto-detect: log all .question elements so we know the ID format */
  var allQ = document.querySelectorAll('.question');
  console.log('[init] All .question IDs:', [].map.call(allQ, function(e){return e.id;}));

  /* ---- hide native Decipher questions ---- */
  ['QS1','QZIP','QAGE','QGENDER','QVOTE24','QS5','QS5A','QS5B'].forEach(function(q){
    var el = findQ(q);
    if(el){
      el.classList.add('sc-native-hidden');
      var radios = el.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
      var texts  = el.querySelectorAll('input[type="text"],input[type="number"]');
      console.log('[init] '+q+' &#8594; id='+el.id+' &#8212; '+radios.length+' radios, '+texts.length+' text inputs');
      if(radios.length) console.log('[init]   values:', [].map.call(radios, function(r){return r.value+' name='+r.name;}));
    } else {
      console.warn('[init] '+q+' NOT FOUND in DOM');
    }
  });

  /* ---- write back to native Decipher inputs ---- */
  function setRadio(q, val){
    var box = findQ(q);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[setRadio] '+q+' NOT FOUND in DOM'); return; }
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    console.log('[setRadio] '+q+' val='+val+' &#8212; found '+all.length+' radios:', [].map.call(all, function(r){return r.value;}));
    /* Position-based first (data-val="1" = 1st radio, etc.), then by value */
    var inp = null;
    var idx = parseInt(val,10);
    if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=all.length) inp = all[idx-1];
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="radio"][value="r'+val+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="radio"][value="'+val+'"]');
    if(inp){
      console.log('[setRadio] '+q+' MATCH &#8594; value='+inp.value+' name='+inp.name);
      inp.checked = true;
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
    } else {
      console.warn('[setRadio] '+q+': NO MATCH for val='+val);
    }
  }
  function setText(q, val){
    var box = findQ(q);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[setText] '+q+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = box.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
    if(inp){
      console.log('[setText] '+q+' &#8594; "'+val+'"');
      inp.value = val;
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
    } else {
      console.warn('[setText] '+q+': no text input found');
    }
  }
  function setNumber(q, val){
    var box = findQ(q);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[setNumber] '+q+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = box.querySelector('input[type="text"],input[type="number"]');
    if(inp){
      console.log('[setNumber] '+q+' &#8594; "'+val+'"');
      inp.value = val;
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
    } else {
      console.warn('[setNumber] '+q+': no input found');
    }
  }

  /* ---- card navigation ---- */
  var LABELS = {
    'card-qs1':'label-qs1','card-qzip':'label-qzip','card-qage':'label-qage',
    'card-qgender':'label-qgender','card-qvote24':'label-qvote24','card-party':'label-party'
  };
  function showCard(idx){
    CARDS.forEach(function(id,i){
      var el = document.getElementById(id);
      if(!el) return;
      var show = i===0 ? idx===0 : i&lt;=idx;
      el.style.display = show ? 'block' : 'none';
      var lbl = LABELS[id] ? document.getElementById(LABELS[id]) : null;
      if(lbl) lbl.style.display = show ? 'block' : 'none';
    });
    updateProgress();
  }
  function advance(){
    if(cur &lt; CARDS.length-1){ cur++; showCard(cur); }
    var last = document.getElementById(CARDS[cur]);
    if(last) last.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'});
  }
  function updateProgress(){
    var wrap = document.getElementById('sc-progress-wrap');
    var fill = document.getElementById('sc-progress-fill');
    var lbl  = document.getElementById('sc-progress-label');
    if(!wrap||!fill) return;
    if(cur&gt;0){
      wrap.style.display='block';
      var pct = Math.round((cur/total)*100);
      fill.style.width = pct+'%';
      if(lbl) lbl.textContent = cur+' of '+total+' Questions';
    }
  }
  function enableNext(){
    jQuery('#sc-continue-wrap').show();
    var wrap = document.getElementById('sc-continue-wrap');
    if(wrap) wrap.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'center'});
  }

  showCard(0);

  /* INTRO */
  jQuery('#sc-start-btn').on('click', function(){ advance(); });

  /* QS1 - registered to vote */
  jQuery('#card-qs1').on('click', '.qs1-btn', function(){
    jQuery('#card-qs1 .qs1-btn').removeClass('sc-sel');
    jQuery(this).addClass('sc-sel');
    setRadio('QS1', jQuery(this).attr('data-val'));
    setTimeout(advance, 350);
  });

  /* ---- validation helpers ---- */
  function showFieldError(id, msg){
    var el = document.getElementById(id);
    if(el){ el.textContent = msg; el.style.display = 'block'; }
  }
  function clearFieldError(id){
    var el = document.getElementById(id);
    if(el){ el.textContent = ''; el.style.display = 'none'; }
  }
  function validateZip(code){
    if(!/^\d{5}$/.test(code)) return 'Please enter a valid 5-digit ZIP code.';
    var pfx = parseInt(code.substring(0,3),10);
    /* US ZIP prefixes run 005-999; gaps: 000-004, 213, 269, 343, 348, 353, 419,
       428-432, 517-519, 529-532, 552, 568, 578, 579, 589, 621, 632, 642, 643,
       659, 663, 731, 732, 742, 771, 817, 818, 819, 839, 848, 849, 854, 858,
       861, 862, 866-869, 876-884, 890-891, 896-899, 929, 952-959, 987 */
    var bad = [0,1,2,3,4,213,269,343,348,353,419,517,518,519,552,568,578,579,
      589,621,632,642,643,659,663,731,732,742,771,817,818,819,839,848,849,
      854,858,861,862,866,867,868,869,876,877,878,879,880,881,882,883,884,
      890,891,896,897,898,899,929,952,953,954,955,956,957,958,959,987];
    if(bad.indexOf(pfx)!==-1) return 'That doesn\u2019t appear to be a valid US ZIP code. Please double-check.';
    return '';
  }
  function validateAge(val){
    var n = parseInt(val,10);
    if(isNaN(n) || n&lt;18) return 'You must be at least 18 to participate.';
    if(n&gt;89) return 'Please enter an age between 18 and 89.';
    return '';
  }

  /* QZIP - zip code digits */
  var zipD = definedAll('#card-qzip .zip-digit');
  jQuery('#card-qzip').on('input', '.zip-digit', function(){
    this.value = this.value.replace(/\D/g,'');
    var idx = zipD.indexOf(this);
    if(this.value.length===1 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;zipD.length-1) zipD[idx+1].focus();
    jQuery(this).toggleClass('zip-filled', this.value.length&gt;0);
    clearFieldError('zip-error');
    jQuery(zipD).removeClass('sc-input-err');
    jQuery('#zip-pna').prop('checked', false);
    var full = jQuery.map(zipD, function(d){return d.value;}).join('');
    if(full.length===5){
      var err = validateZip(full);
      if(err){
        showFieldError('zip-error', err);
        jQuery(zipD).addClass('sc-input-err');
      } else {
        setText('QZIP', full);
        setTimeout(advance, 400);
      }
    }
  });
  jQuery('#card-qzip').on('keydown', '.zip-digit', function(e){
    var idx = zipD.indexOf(this);
    if(e.key==='Backspace' &amp;&amp; !this.value &amp;&amp; idx&gt;0) zipD[idx-1].focus();
  });
  jQuery('#zip-pna').on('change', function(){
    if(this.checked){
      jQuery(zipD).val('').prop('disabled',true).removeClass('zip-filled sc-input-err');
      clearFieldError('zip-error');
      setText('QZIP','');
      setTimeout(advance, 350);
    } else { jQuery(zipD).prop('disabled',false); }
  });
  jQuery('.zip-why-trigger').on('click', function(){
    jQuery('.zip-why-body').toggle();
  });

  /* QAGE - age digits */
  var ageD = definedAll('#card-qage .age-digit');
  jQuery('#card-qage').on('input', '.age-digit', function(){
    this.value = this.value.replace(/\D/g,'');
    var idx = ageD.indexOf(this);
    if(this.value.length===1 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;ageD.length-1) ageD[idx+1].focus();
    jQuery(this).toggleClass('age-filled', this.value.length&gt;0);
    clearFieldError('age-error');
    jQuery(ageD).removeClass('sc-input-err');
    jQuery('#age-pna').prop('checked', false);
    var full = jQuery.map(ageD, function(d){return d.value;}).join('');
    if(full.length===2){
      var err = validateAge(full);
      if(err){
        showFieldError('age-error', err);
        jQuery(ageD).addClass('sc-input-err');
      } else {
        setNumber('QAGE', full);
        setTimeout(advance, 400);
      }
    }
  });
  jQuery('#card-qage').on('keydown', '.age-digit', function(e){
    var idx = ageD.indexOf(this);
    if(e.key==='Backspace' &amp;&amp; !this.value &amp;&amp; idx&gt;0) ageD[idx-1].focus();
  });
  jQuery('#age-pna').on('change', function(){
    if(this.checked){
      jQuery(ageD).val('').prop('disabled',true).removeClass('age-filled sc-input-err');
      clearFieldError('age-error');
      setNumber('QAGE','');
      setTimeout(advance, 350);
    } else { jQuery(ageD).prop('disabled',false); }
  });

  /* QGENDER - horizontal pills */
  jQuery('#gender-pills').on('click', '.gender-pill', function(){
    jQuery('#gender-pills .gender-pill').removeClass('sc-sel');
    jQuery(this).addClass('sc-sel');
    jQuery('#gender-pna').prop('checked', false);
    setRadio('QGENDER', jQuery(this).attr('data-val'));

  jQuery('#gender-pna').on('change', function(){

  /* QVOTE24 - custom ballot */
  jQuery('#ballot-vote24').on('click', '.ballot-row, .ballot-bottom-row', function(){
    jQuery('#ballot-vote24 .ballot-row, #ballot-vote24 .ballot-bottom-row').removeClass('sc-sel');

  /* QS5 / QS5A / QS5B - party identification */
  var partyChoice = '';
  jQuery('#card-party').on('click', '.party-main-btn', function(){
    jQuery('#card-party .party-main-btn').removeClass('sc-sel');
    jQuery(this).addClass('sc-sel');
    jQuery('#party-pna').prop('checked', false);
    var v = jQuery(this).attr('data-val');
    partyChoice = v;
    setRadio('QS5', v);
    jQuery('#party-pna-main').hide();
    if(v==='1'||v==='2'){
      jQuery('#party-sub-a').show();
      jQuery('#qs5a-pipe').text(v==='1' ? 'Republican' : 'Democrat');
      jQuery('#pill-gop').removeClass('sc-active sc-dim');
      jQuery('#pill-dem').removeClass('sc-active sc-dim');
      if(v==='1'){ jQuery('#pill-gop').addClass('sc-active'); jQuery('#pill-dem').addClass('sc-dim'); }
      else { jQuery('#pill-dem').addClass('sc-active'); jQuery('#pill-gop').addClass('sc-dim'); }
      jQuery('#party-sub-b').hide();
    } else {
      jQuery('#party-sub-a').hide();
      jQuery('#party-sub-b').show();
    }
  });
  jQuery('#party-sub-a').on('click', '.party-sub-radio', function(){
    jQuery('#party-sub-a .party-sub-radio').removeClass('sc-sel');
    jQuery(this).addClass('sc-sel');
    jQuery('#party2-pna').prop('checked', false);
    setRadio('QS5A', jQuery(this).attr('data-val'));
    enableNext();
  });
  jQuery('#party2-pna').on('change', function(){
    if(this.checked){ enableNext(); }
  });
  jQuery('#party-sub-b').on('click', '.party-lean-btn', function(){
    jQuery('#party-sub-b .party-lean-btn').removeClass('sc-sel');
    jQuery(this).addClass('sc-sel');
    jQuery('#party3-pna').prop('checked', false);
    setRadio('QS5B', jQuery(this).attr('data-val'));
    enableNext();
  });
  jQuery('#party3-pna').on('change', function(){
    if(this.checked){ enableNext(); }
  });
  jQuery('#party-pna').on('change', function(){
    if(this.checked){ enableNext(); }
  });

  /* CONTINUE button &#8212; validate then trigger native Decipher page submit */
  jQuery('#sc-continue-btn').on('click', function(){
    /* Re-validate ZIP and age before submitting */
    var zipVal = jQuery.map(zipD, function(d){return d.value;}).join('');
    var ageVal = jQuery.map(ageD, function(d){return d.value;}).join('');
    var blocked = false;

    if(zipVal.length &amp;&amp; zipVal.length===5){
      var ze = validateZip(zipVal);
      if(ze){ showFieldError('zip-error',ze); jQuery(zipD).addClass('sc-input-err'); blocked=true; }
    }
    if(ageVal.length &amp;&amp; ageVal.length===2){
      var ae = validateAge(ageVal);
      if(ae){ showFieldError('age-error',ae); jQuery(ageD).addClass('sc-input-err'); blocked=true; }
    }
    if(blocked){
      var errEl = document.querySelector('.sc-field-error[style*="block"]');
      if(errEl) errEl.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'center'});
      return;
    }

    console.log('[CONTINUE] clicked &#8212; dumping native input states:');
    ['QS1','QZIP','QAGE','QGENDER','QVOTE24','QS5','QS5A','QS5B'].forEach(function(q){
      var box = findQ(q);
      if(!box){ console.log('  '+q+': NOT IN DOM'); return; }
      var checked = box.querySelector('input[type="radio"]:checked');
      var text = box.querySelector('input[type="text"],input[type="number"]');
      if(checked) console.log('  '+q+': radio='+checked.value);
      else if(text) console.log('  '+q+': text="'+text.value+'"');
      else console.log('  '+q+': (no selection)');
    });
    /* Override !important by adding inline style with !important via setAttribute */
    var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
    if(nxt){
      nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
      console.log('[CONTINUE] native button found, clicking:', nxt.tagName, nxt.className);
      nxt.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[CONTINUE] NO native submit button found &#8212; trying form submit');
      var form = document.querySelector('form');
      if(form) form.submit();
    }
  });

  /* Surface Decipher server-side validation errors on hidden native questions */
  jQuery(function(){
    var nativeErrs = jQuery('.question.sc-native-hidden .error, .question.sc-native-hidden .cell.error');
    if(nativeErrs.length){
      nativeErrs.each(function(){
        var qEl = jQuery(this).closest('.question');
        var qId = qEl.attr('id') || '';
        if(qId.indexOf('ZIP')!==-1||qId.indexOf('zip')!==-1){
          showFieldError('zip-error', jQuery(this).text().trim() || 'Please enter a valid ZIP code.');
          jQuery(zipD).addClass('sc-input-err');
        }
        if(qId.indexOf('AGE')!==-1||qId.indexOf('age')!==-1){
          showFieldError('age-error', jQuery(this).text().trim() || 'Please enter a valid age.');
          jQuery(ageD).addClass('sc-input-err');
        }
      });
      var errEl = document.querySelector('.sc-field-error[style*="block"]');
      if(errEl) errEl.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'center'});
    }
  });

def setupMaxDiffFile(fname, fileDelimiter="\t"):
    try:
        f = open("%s/%s" % (gv.survey.path, fname))
        mdObj = [ line.strip("\r\n").split(fileDelimiter) for line in f.readlines() ]
        d = dict( ("v%s_t%s" % (row[0], row[1]), row[2:]) for row in mdObj )
    except IOError:
        d = {}
    return d
def setupMaxDiffItemsI(d, vt, question):
    item_index = dict( (r.o.label.strip("item"), r.index) for r in question.rows )
    if vt not in d:
        raise Exception("MaxDiff design key '%s' not found. Available keys: %s" % (vt, ", ".join(sorted(d.keys())[:20])))
    items = d[vt]
    for r in question.rows:
        if r.o.label.strip("item") not in items:
            r.disabled = True
    question.rows.order = [ item_index[i] for i in items ]
    print "*****STAFF ONLY*****"
    print "Version_Task: %s" % vt
    for i in range(len(items)):
        print "Item %s: %s" % (i+1,items[i])
        p.maxdiff1.append(items[i])
</exec><suspend/><exec>

party = 4
if QS5.r1:
    party = 1 if QS5A.r1 else 2
elif QS5.r2:
    party = 7 if QS5A.r1 else 6
elif QS5.r3 or QS5.r4:
    if QS5B.r1:   party = 3
    elif QS5B.r2: party = 5
    else:          party = 4

    if party &lt;= 3:
        TYPING_MODULE.val = TYPING_MODULE.r1.index
    else:
        TYPING_MODULE.val = TYPING_MODULE.r3.index
elif QVOTE24.r2:
    if party &gt;= 5:
        TYPING_MODULE.val = TYPING_MODULE.r2.index
    else:
        TYPING_MODULE.val = TYPING_MODULE.r3.index

&lt;script&gt;
(function(){
  /* set progress bar width from Decipher template vars */
  var pFill = document.getElementById('md-progress-fill');
  if(pFill){
    var curCard = parseInt('${p.MDcount}',10) || 1;
    var totalCards = parseInt('${len(QMD1_md_loop_expanded.order)}',10) || 1;
    pFill.style.width = Math.round((curCard/totalCards)*100)+'%';
  }

  var q = document.querySelector('.QMD1_maxdiff');
  if(!q) return;

  var allRadios = [].slice.call(q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]'));
  var groups = {};
  allRadios.forEach(function(r){ (groups[r.name] = groups[r.name]||[]).push(r); });
  var gnames = Object.keys(groups);
  console.log('[MD-DEM] radio groups found:', gnames);
  if(gnames.length &lt; 2){ console.warn('[MD-DEM] need 2+ radio groups'); return; }

  var bestRadios = groups[gnames[0]];
  var worstRadios = groups[gnames[1]];
  console.log('[MD-DEM] best:', bestRadios.length, 'worst:', worstRadios.length);

  var items = [];
  bestRadios.forEach(function(r,i){
    var row = r.closest('tr, .row-element, .row, label, li');
    var text = '';
    if(row){
      var legend = row.querySelector('th.row-legend, td.row-legend, .row-legend-text, .row-legend');
      if(!legend) legend = row.querySelector('.text');
      text = legend ? legend.textContent.trim() : '';
      if(!text){
        var clone = row.cloneNode(true);
        clone.querySelectorAll('input,th.col-legend,td.col-legend').forEach(function(el){ el.remove(); });
        text = clone.textContent.trim();
      }
    }
    if(!text) text = 'Statement '+(i+1);
    /* strip any [label] prefix from Decipher row text */
    var bi = text.indexOf(']');
    if(bi &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; bi &lt; 30) text = text.substring(bi+1).trim();
    console.log('[MD-DEM] item'+i+' text:', JSON.stringify(text));
    items.push(text);
  });

  var wrap = document.createElement('div');
  wrap.className = 'md-custom-ui';
  wrap.innerHTML = '&lt;div class="md-header-row"&gt;' +
    '&lt;span class="md-header-most"&gt;MOST&lt;br&gt;LIKE ME&lt;/span&gt;' +
    '&lt;span class="md-header-least"&gt;LEAST&lt;br&gt;LIKE ME&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';

  var bestSel = -1, worstSel = -1;

  function updateUI(){
    var rows = wrap.querySelectorAll('.md-row');
    var allBest = wrap.querySelectorAll('.md-radio-best');
    var allWorst = wrap.querySelectorAll('.md-radio-worst');
    for(var i=0;i&lt;rows.length;i++){
      rows[i].classList.remove('md-has-best','md-has-worst');
      allBest[i].classList.remove('md-best-checked');
      allWorst[i].classList.remove('md-worst-checked');
      if(i===bestSel){ rows[i].classList.add('md-has-best'); allBest[i].classList.add('md-best-checked'); }
      if(i===worstSel){ rows[i].classList.add('md-has-worst'); allWorst[i].classList.add('md-worst-checked'); }
    }
    var btn = document.getElementById('md-continue-btn');
    if(btn){
      if(bestSel&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; worstSel&gt;=0){ btn.style.opacity='1'; btn.style.pointerEvents='auto'; }
      else { btn.style.opacity='.4'; btn.style.pointerEvents='none'; }
    }
  }

  items.forEach(function(txt,i){
    var row = document.createElement('div');
    row.className = 'md-row';
    row.innerHTML = '&lt;button type="button" class="md-radio md-radio-best" data-idx="'+i+'"&gt;&lt;/button&gt;' +
      '&lt;div class="md-row-text"&gt;'+txt+'&lt;/div&gt;' +
      '&lt;button type="button" class="md-radio md-radio-worst" data-idx="'+i+'"&gt;&lt;/button&gt;';
    wrap.appendChild(row);
  });

  wrap.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    var btn = e.target.closest('.md-radio');
    if(!btn) return;
    var idx = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-idx'),10);
    if(btn.classList.contains('md-radio-best')){
      if(idx===worstSel) return;
      bestSel = (bestSel===idx) ? -1 : idx;
      if(bestSel&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; bestRadios[bestSel]){ bestRadios[bestSel].checked=true; bestRadios[bestSel].click(); }
    } else {
      if(idx===bestSel) return;
      worstSel = (worstSel===idx) ? -1 : idx;
      if(worstSel&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; worstRadios[worstSel]){ worstRadios[worstSel].checked=true; worstRadios[worstSel].click(); }
    }
    updateUI();
  });

  q.insertBefore(wrap, q.firstChild);

  var btn = document.getElementById('md-continue-btn');
  if(btn){
    btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(bestSel&lt;0||worstSel&lt;0) return;
      var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
      if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
      if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
      } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
      }
    });
  }
})();
&lt;/script&gt;

&lt;script&gt;
(function(){
  /* --- find native radios for both questions --- */
  var boxes = document.querySelectorAll('.vec_dem_q');
  if(boxes.length &lt; 2) return;

  var questions = [];
  boxes.forEach(function(box){
    var radios = [].slice.call(box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]'));
    var row = box.querySelector('th.row-legend, td.row-legend, .row-legend-text, .row-legend, .text');
    var text = row ? row.textContent.trim() : '';
    if(!text){
      /* fallback: get from row element text */
      var rowEl = box.querySelector('.row-elements, .row-element, tr.row');
      if(rowEl){
        var clone = rowEl.cloneNode(true);
        clone.querySelectorAll('input,th.col-legend,td.col-legend').forEach(function(el){ el.remove(); });
        text = clone.textContent.trim();
      }
    }
    /* strip any [label] prefix */
    var bi = text.indexOf(']');
    if(bi &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; bi &lt; 30) text = text.substring(bi+1).trim();
    questions.push({ radios: radios, text: text || 'Statement' });
  });

  /* --- build custom UI --- */
  var card = document.querySelector('.vec-card');
  if(!card) return;
  var preferWrap = card.querySelector('.vec-prefer-wrap');

  var selections = [-1, -1]; /* index of selected dot per question */

  function updateContinue(){
    var btn = document.getElementById('vec-continue-btn');
    var skip = document.getElementById('vec-prefer-skip');
    if(!btn) return;
    var allDone = (selections[0] &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; selections[1] &gt;= 0);
    var skipped = skip &amp;&amp; skip.checked;
    if(allDone || skipped){
      btn.style.opacity = '1'; btn.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
    } else {
      btn.style.opacity = '.4'; btn.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
    }
  }

  questions.forEach(function(qObj, qi){
    var item = document.createElement('div');
    item.className = 'vec-item';
    item.innerHTML = '&lt;div class="vec-item-text"&gt;' + qObj.text + '&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="vec-dots"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;' +
      '&lt;div class="vec-dot-labels"&gt;&lt;span&gt;Strongly Disagree&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Neutral&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Strongly Agree&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
    var dotsWrap = item.querySelector('.vec-dots');

    for(var d = 0; d &lt; 7; d++){
      var dot = document.createElement('button');
      dot.type = 'button';
      dot.className = 'vec-dot';
      dot.setAttribute('data-qi', qi);
      dot.setAttribute('data-di', d);
      dotsWrap.appendChild(dot);
    }

    dotsWrap.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      var dot = e.target.closest('.vec-dot');
      if(!dot) return;
      var di = parseInt(dot.getAttribute('data-di'), 10);
      /* toggle off if same dot clicked */
      if(selections[qi] === di){
        selections[qi] = -1;
      } else {
        selections[qi] = di;
        /* sync to native radio */
        if(qObj.radios[di]){
          qObj.radios[di].checked = true;
          qObj.radios[di].click();
        }
      }
      /* update dot visuals &#8212; color by position */
      var allDots = dotsWrap.querySelectorAll('.vec-dot');
      var cnames = ['vec-c1','vec-c2','vec-c3','vec-c4','vec-c5','vec-c6','vec-c7'];
      allDots.forEach(function(dd, idx){
        cnames.forEach(function(cn){ dd.classList.remove(cn); });
        if(idx === selections[qi]) dd.classList.add(cnames[idx]);
      });
      /* uncheck prefer-not-to-respond when a dot is selected */
      var skip = document.getElementById('vec-prefer-skip');
      if(skip) skip.checked = false;
      updateContinue();
    });

    /* insert items BEFORE the prefer-not checkbox */
    if(preferWrap){
      card.insertBefore(item, preferWrap);
    } else {
      card.appendChild(item);
    }
  });

  /* --- prefer-not-to-respond checkbox --- */
  var skip = document.getElementById('vec-prefer-skip');
  if(skip){
    skip.addEventListener('change', function(){
      if(skip.checked){
        /* clear selections visually */
        var cnames = ['vec-c1','vec-c2','vec-c3','vec-c4','vec-c5','vec-c6','vec-c7'];
        card.querySelectorAll('.vec-dot').forEach(function(d){ cnames.forEach(function(cn){ d.classList.remove(cn); }); });
        selections = [-1, -1];
        /* set native radios to neutral (c4) as default for skippers */
        questions.forEach(function(qObj){
          if(qObj.radios[3]){ qObj.radios[3].checked = true; qObj.radios[3].click(); }
        });
      }
      updateContinue();
    });
  }

  /* --- continue button --- */
  var btn = document.getElementById('vec-continue-btn');
  if(btn){
    btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage');
      if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('input.button');
      if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
      } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
      }
    });
  }
})();

import math

def centroidDistance(resp_answers, segment_coeff):
    return sum((a - c)**2 for a, c in zip(resp_answers, segment_coeff))

def centroidAllSegments(answers, centroid_matrix):
    num_segments = len(centroid_matrix[0])
    d2_list = []
    for c in range(num_segments):
        segment_col = [row[c] for row in centroid_matrix]
        d2_list.append(centroidDistance(answers, segment_col))
    return d2_list

p.dem_z = [float(XDEM_SEG.rows[i].c4.val) for i in range(10)]
p.dem_z.append(float(XDEM_SEG.r13.c4.val))
p.dem_z.append(float(XDEM_SEG.r14.c4.val))

dem_centroids = [
    [-0.5135, -0.1429, -0.3291, 0.544, 0.9293, -0.3204],
    [-0.039, -0.8206, -0.544, 0.1583, 0.6292, 0.8164],
    [-0.4356, -0.3798, -0.3126, 1.1914, 0.6485, -0.4382],
    [0.4891, -0.5913, 0.7544, 0.2422, -0.1966, -0.7195],
    [0.5194, 0.2926, 0.2316, 0.1168, -1.3929, 0.1419],
    [-0.1269, -0.1611, 0.5696, -0.2886, -0.2956, 0.2223],
    [0.257, 0.8708, -0.2005, -0.5704, -0.3712, -0.1654],
    [0.4032, -0.1316, 0.0902, -0.9386, -0.1134, 0.547],
    [-0.7075, 1.0908, -0.1312, 0.2406, 0.0411, -0.5795],
    [0.1626, -0.2097, -0.1184, -0.7095, 0.2866, 0.5285],
    [0.7218, 0.4355, -0.4757, -0.3332, -0.4753, 0.2212],
    [0.7961, 0.1727, 0.0062, -0.267, -0.5004, -0.0547]
]

p.dem_d2 = centroidAllSegments(p.dem_z, dem_centroids)

p.dem_exp = [math.exp(-d/2.0) for d in p.dem_d2]
dem_exp_sum = sum(p.dem_exp)
p.dem_prob = [(e/dem_exp_sum)*100.0 for e in p.dem_exp]

for i in range(6):
    XDEM_SOFTMAX.rows[i].c1.val = round(p.dem_d2[i], 4)
    XDEM_SOFTMAX.rows[i].c2.val = round(p.dem_exp[i], 6)
    XDEM_SOFTMAX.rows[i].c3.val = round(p.dem_prob[i], 2)

sorted_probs = sorted(enumerate(p.dem_prob), key=lambda x: -x[1])
XDEM_SEG_FINAL_1.val = XDEM_SEG_FINAL_1.rows[sorted_probs[0][0]].index
XDEM_SEG_FINAL_2.val = XDEM_SEG_FINAL_2.rows[sorted_probs[1][0]].index

gap = sorted_probs[0][1] - sorted_probs[1][1]
XDEM_CONFIDENCE.r1.val = round(sorted_probs[0][1], 2)
XDEM_CONFIDENCE.r2.val = round(sorted_probs[1][1], 2)
XDEM_CONFIDENCE.r3.val = round(gap, 2)
entropy_val = -sum((pr/100.0)*math.log(pr/100.0+1e-12) for pr in p.dem_prob)
XDEM_CONFIDENCE.r4.val = round(entropy_val, 4)

&lt;script&gt;
(function(){
  /* set progress bar width from Decipher template vars */
  var pFill = document.getElementById('md-progress-fill-gop');
  if(pFill){
    var curCard = parseInt('${p.MDcount}',10) || 1;
    var totalCards = parseInt('${len(QMD3_md_loop_expanded.order)}',10) || 1;
    pFill.style.width = Math.round((curCard/totalCards)*100)+'%';
  }

  var q = document.querySelector('.QMD3_maxdiff');
  if(!q) return;

  /* find all native radio inputs grouped by column (best/worst) */
  var bestRadios = [].slice.call(q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"][name*="_best_"],input[type="radio"][name*=".best."],input[type="radio"][name*="c1"]'));
  var worstRadios = [].slice.call(q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"][name*="_worst_"],input[type="radio"][name*=".worst."],input[type="radio"][name*="c2"]'));

  /* fallback: if can't find by name pattern, find by grouping structure */
  if(!bestRadios.length || !worstRadios.length){
    var allRadios = [].slice.call(q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]'));
    /* group by name attribute */
    var groups = {};
    allRadios.forEach(function(r){ (groups[r.name] = groups[r.name]||[]).push(r); });
    var gnames = Object.keys(groups);
    console.log('[MD-GOP] radio groups found:', gnames);
    if(gnames.length &gt;= 2){
      /* first group = best, second = worst */
      bestRadios = groups[gnames[0]];
      worstRadios = groups[gnames[1]];
    }
  }

  if(!bestRadios.length || !worstRadios.length){
    console.warn('[MD-GOP] could not find best/worst radios');
    return;
  }

  console.log('[MD-GOP] best:', bestRadios.length, 'worst:', worstRadios.length);

  /* extract item labels from the native rendering */
  var items = [];
  bestRadios.forEach(function(r,i){
    var row = r.closest('tr, .row-element, .row, label, li');
    var text = '';
    if(row){
      var legend = row.querySelector('th.row-legend, td.row-legend, .row-legend-text, .row-legend');
      if(!legend) legend = row.querySelector('.text');
      text = legend ? legend.textContent.trim() : '';
      if(!text){
        var clone = row.cloneNode(true);
        clone.querySelectorAll('input,th.col-legend,td.col-legend').forEach(function(el){ el.remove(); });
        text = clone.textContent.trim();
      }
    }
    if(!text) text = 'Statement '+(i+1);
    /* strip any [label] prefix from Decipher row text */
    var bi = text.indexOf(']');
    if(bi &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; bi &lt; 30) text = text.substring(bi+1).trim();
    console.log('[MD-GOP] item'+i+' text:', JSON.stringify(text));
    items.push(text);
  });

  /* build custom UI */
  var wrap = document.createElement('div');
  wrap.className = 'md-custom-ui';
  wrap.innerHTML = '&lt;div class="md-header-row"&gt;' +
    '&lt;span class="md-header-most"&gt;MOST&lt;br&gt;LIKE ME&lt;/span&gt;' +
    '&lt;span class="md-header-least"&gt;LEAST&lt;br&gt;LIKE ME&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';

  var bestSel = -1, worstSel = -1;

  function updateUI(){
    var rows = wrap.querySelectorAll('.md-row');
    var allBest = wrap.querySelectorAll('.md-radio-best');
    var allWorst = wrap.querySelectorAll('.md-radio-worst');
    for(var i=0;i&lt;rows.length;i++){
      rows[i].classList.remove('md-has-best','md-has-worst');
      allBest[i].classList.remove('md-best-checked');
      allWorst[i].classList.remove('md-worst-checked');
      if(i===bestSel){ rows[i].classList.add('md-has-best'); allBest[i].classList.add('md-best-checked'); }
      if(i===worstSel){ rows[i].classList.add('md-has-worst'); allWorst[i].classList.add('md-worst-checked'); }
    }
    /* enable continue only when both selected */
    var btn = document.getElementById('md-continue-btn');
    if(btn){
      if(bestSel&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; worstSel&gt;=0){ btn.style.opacity='1'; btn.style.pointerEvents='auto'; }
      else { btn.style.opacity='.4'; btn.style.pointerEvents='none'; }
    }
  }

  items.forEach(function(txt,i){
    var row = document.createElement('div');
    row.className = 'md-row';
    row.innerHTML = '&lt;button type="button" class="md-radio md-radio-best" data-idx="'+i+'"&gt;&lt;/button&gt;' +
      '&lt;div class="md-row-text"&gt;'+txt+'&lt;/div&gt;' +
      '&lt;button type="button" class="md-radio md-radio-worst" data-idx="'+i+'"&gt;&lt;/button&gt;';
    wrap.appendChild(row);
  });

  /* click handlers */
  wrap.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    var btn = e.target.closest('.md-radio');
    if(!btn) return;
    var idx = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-idx'),10);
    if(btn.classList.contains('md-radio-best')){
      if(idx===worstSel) return; /* can't pick same row */
      bestSel = (bestSel===idx) ? -1 : idx;
      /* sync to native radio */
      if(bestSel&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; bestRadios[bestSel]){ bestRadios[bestSel].checked=true; bestRadios[bestSel].click(); }
    } else {
      if(idx===bestSel) return;
      worstSel = (worstSel===idx) ? -1 : idx;
      if(worstSel&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; worstRadios[worstSel]){ worstRadios[worstSel].checked=true; worstRadios[worstSel].click(); }
    }
    updateUI();
  });

  /* insert custom UI before the native question */
  q.insertBefore(wrap, q.firstChild);

  /* continue button */
  var btn = document.getElementById('md-continue-btn');
  if(btn){
    btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(bestSel&lt;0||worstSel&lt;0) return;
      var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
      if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
      if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
      } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
      }
    });
  }
})();
&lt;/script&gt;

import math

def centroidDistance(resp_answers, segment_coeff):
    return sum((a - c)**2 for a, c in zip(resp_answers, segment_coeff))

def centroidAllSegments(answers, centroid_matrix):
    num_segments = len(centroid_matrix[0])
    d2_list = []
    for c in range(num_segments):
        segment_col = [row[c] for row in centroid_matrix]
        d2_list.append(centroidDistance(answers, segment_col))
    return d2_list

p.gop_z = [float(x) for x in XGOP_SEG.c4.values]

gop_centroids = [
    [0.2, 0.0096, 0.9146, -0.1336, -0.6956, 0.5846, 0.4648, -0.2554, -0.739, -0.8787],
    [-0.0608, 0.0308, -0.5647, 0.0053, 0.7257, -0.0362, 0.0185, -0.4401, 0.1704, 0.6758],
    [-0.0633, 0.67, -0.4791, -0.3529, 0.712, -0.2058, -0.5104, -0.4564, 0.3953, 0.0561],
    [0.8912, 0.4863, -0.2283, 0.1686, 0.9888, -0.7418, -0.9072, 0.1943, -0.1989, -0.4581],
    [0.1561, -0.7521, -0.6867, 0.6036, -0.1513, -0.0754, 0.8258, 0.3333, -0.0793, 1.0337],
    [-0.6021, 0.1277, -0.2994, 0.0551, 0.2664, -0.4837, -0.1493, 0.1478, 0.5757, 0.4379],
    [-0.1778, -0.9908, -0.8135, 0.233, -0.1464, 0.0851, 0.236, 0.9657, 0.3877, 0.9297],
    [-0.7705, -0.2343, -0.3477, -1.0279, -0.572, 0.6932, 0.1564, 0.2632, 0.5845, 0.5142],
    [0.1964, -0.5763, 0.0446, 1.363, -0.0369, -0.4206, 0.9004, 0.2931, -0.5885, 0.1112],
    [-0.3176, 0.7097, 0.4794, -0.8491, -0.2762, 0.4546, -0.4476, -0.8232, 0.3467, -0.4787],
    [0.5922, 0.291, 1.1052, 0.6792, 0.0203, -0.5188, -0.4748, 0.0904, -0.7155, -1.192],
    [-0.0166, 0.3879, 0.9236, -0.8652, -0.687, 0.6888, -0.2467, -0.4652, -0.1536, -0.8748]
]

p.gop_d2 = centroidAllSegments(p.gop_z, gop_centroids)

p.gop_exp = [math.exp(-d/2.0) for d in p.gop_d2]
gop_exp_sum = sum(p.gop_exp)
p.gop_prob = [(e/gop_exp_sum)*100.0 for e in p.gop_exp]

for i in range(10):
    XGOP_SOFTMAX.rows[i].c1.val = round(p.gop_d2[i], 4)
    XGOP_SOFTMAX.rows[i].c2.val = round(p.gop_exp[i], 6)
    XGOP_SOFTMAX.rows[i].c3.val = round(p.gop_prob[i], 2)

sorted_probs = sorted(enumerate(p.gop_prob), key=lambda x: -x[1])
XGOP_SEG_FINAL_1.val = XGOP_SEG_FINAL_1.rows[sorted_probs[0][0]].index
XGOP_SEG_FINAL_2.val = XGOP_SEG_FINAL_2.rows[sorted_probs[1][0]].index

gap = sorted_probs[0][1] - sorted_probs[1][1]
XGOP_CONFIDENCE.r1.val = round(sorted_probs[0][1], 2)
XGOP_CONFIDENCE.r2.val = round(sorted_probs[1][1], 2)
XGOP_CONFIDENCE.r3.val = round(gap, 2)
entropy_val = -sum((pr/100.0)*math.log(pr/100.0+1e-12) for pr in p.gop_prob)
XGOP_CONFIDENCE.r4.val = round(entropy_val, 4)

&lt;script&gt;
(function(){
  /* Guard: only run on INF1 page */
  if(!document.getElementById('inf1-card')) return;

  /* ---- find Decipher question element by label ---- */
  function findQ(q){
    var el = document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]');
    /* If we found an input rather than the question container, walk up */
    if(el &amp;&amp; el.closest &amp;&amp; !el.classList.contains('question')){
      var par = el.closest('.question');
      if(par) el = par;
    }
    return el;
  }

  /* ---- Debug: log all .question elements + their inputs ---- */
  var allQ = document.querySelectorAll('.question');
  console.log('[INF1 init] All .question IDs:', [].map.call(allQ, function(e){return e.id;}));
  var infBox = findQ('INF1');
  if(infBox){
    console.log('[INF1 init] Found INF1 id='+infBox.id);
    var allInputs = infBox.querySelectorAll('input');
    console.log('[INF1 init] INF1 has '+allInputs.length+' inputs:');
    [].forEach.call(allInputs, function(inp){
      console.log('  type='+inp.type+' name='+inp.name+' value='+inp.value+' checked='+inp.checked);
    });
  } else {
    console.warn('[INF1 init] INF1 NOT FOUND - dumping all questions with checkboxes:');
    allQ.forEach(function(q){
      var cbs = q.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      if(cbs.length &gt; 0){
        console.log('  '+q.id+' has '+cbs.length+' checkboxes');
        [].forEach.call(cbs, function(cb){
          console.log('    name='+cb.name+' value='+cb.value);
        });
      }
    });
  }

  /* ---- sync checkbox to native Decipher input ---- */
  function syncCheckbox(qLabel, rowLabel, checked){
    var box = findQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[syncCB] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;

    /* Strategy 1: value matches row label */
    inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][value="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    /* Strategy 2: name contains row label */
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name*="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    /* Strategy 3: position-based (r1=1st checkbox, r2=2nd, etc.) */
    if(!inp){
      var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(m){
        var idx = parseInt(m[1], 10);
        var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
        if(idx === 99){
          /* r99 = exclusive/noanswer = usually last checkbox */
          for(var k=0; k&lt;allCB.length; k++){
            var nm = (allCB[k].name||'')+(allCB[k].className||'');
            if(nm.indexOf('noanswer')!==-1||nm.indexOf('exclusive')!==-1){inp=allCB[k]; break;}
          }
          if(!inp &amp;&amp; allCB.length&gt;0) inp = allCB[allCB.length-1];
        } else if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=allCB.length){
          inp = allCB[idx-1];
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 4: scan ALL inputs */
    if(!inp){
      var all2 = box.querySelectorAll('input');
      for(var j=0; j&lt;all2.length; j++){
        if(all2[j].value===rowLabel||(all2[j].name&amp;&amp;all2[j].name.indexOf(rowLabel)!==-1)){inp=all2[j]; break;}
      }
    }

    if(inp){
      console.log('[syncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' checked='+checked+' (name='+inp.name+' val='+inp.value+' type='+inp.type+')');
      if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[syncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' NO INPUT FOUND in #'+box.id);
    }
  }

  /* ---- state tracking ---- */
  var selected = {};
  var noneSelected = false;

  var checkRows = document.querySelectorAll('#inf1-checks .inf-check-row');
  var noneBtn = document.getElementById('inf1-none');
  var continueBtn = document.getElementById('inf1-continue');

  function updateContinue(){
    var anyChecked = Object.keys(selected).some(function(k){ return selected[k]; });
    continueBtn.disabled = !(anyChecked || noneSelected);
  }

  /* Checkbox row click */
  checkRows.forEach(function(row){
    row.addEventListener('click', function(){
      var r = row.getAttribute('data-row');
      selected[r] = !selected[r];
      row.classList.toggle('inf-checked', selected[r]);
      syncCheckbox('INF1', r, selected[r]);

      if(selected[r] &amp;&amp; noneSelected){
        noneSelected = false;
        noneBtn.classList.remove('inf-sel');
        syncCheckbox('INF1', 'r99', false);
      }
      updateContinue();
    });
  });

  /* None of these click */
  noneBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    noneSelected = !noneSelected;
    noneBtn.classList.toggle('inf-sel', noneSelected);
    syncCheckbox('INF1', 'r99', noneSelected);

    if(noneSelected){
      checkRows.forEach(function(row){
        var r = row.getAttribute('data-row');
        selected[r] = false;
        row.classList.remove('inf-checked');
        syncCheckbox('INF1', r, false);
      });
    }
    updateContinue();
  });

  /* Continue button */
  continueBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    if(continueBtn.disabled) return;
    console.log('[INF1 SUBMIT] selected=', JSON.stringify(selected), 'none=', noneSelected);

    /* Verify native inputs */
    var box = findQ('INF1');
    if(box){
      var chkd = box.querySelectorAll('input:checked');
      console.log('[INF1 SUBMIT] Native checked: '+chkd.length);
      [].forEach.call(chkd, function(c){ console.log('  '+c.name+'='+c.value); });

      /* Emergency fallback: if nothing checked natively, force-set by position */
      if(chkd.length === 0){
        console.warn('[INF1 SUBMIT] FALLBACK: force-setting by position');
        var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
        console.log('[INF1 SUBMIT] Found '+allCB.length+' native checkboxes');
        Object.keys(selected).forEach(function(r){
          if(!selected[r]) return;
          var m2 = r.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
          if(m2){
            var i2 = parseInt(m2[1],10) - 1;
            if(i2 &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; i2 &lt; allCB.length){
              allCB[i2].checked = true;
              allCB[i2].click();
              try{ jQuery(allCB[i2]).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
              console.log('[INF1 SUBMIT] Force-set idx='+i2+' name='+allCB[i2].name);
            }
          }
        });
        if(noneSelected &amp;&amp; allCB.length &gt; 0){
          var last = allCB[allCB.length-1];
          last.checked = true; last.click();
          try{ jQuery(last).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
          console.log('[INF1 SUBMIT] Force-set None (last)');
        }
      }
    }

    var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
    if(nxt){
      nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
      console.log('[INF1 SUBMIT] Clicking native button:', nxt.tagName, nxt.className);
      nxt.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[INF1 SUBMIT] No native button - form.submit()');
      var form = document.querySelector('form');
      if(form) form.submit();
    }
  });
})();
&lt;/script&gt;

  &lt;div class="inf-q-label"&gt;4 of 4 Questions&lt;/div&gt;

    &lt;div class="inf-q-title"&gt;How many times over the past 30 days have you&amp;hellip;&lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;div class="inf-q-subtitle"&gt;Across social media platforms you use (X/Twitter, Instagram, TikTok, Facebook, Substack, YouTube, etc.). Approximately how many times have you done any of the following to advocate on a public policy issue?&lt;/div&gt;

    &lt;div class="inf-swipe-wrap" id="inf8-swipe"&gt;
      &lt;div class="inf-swipe-peek"&gt;
        &lt;span class="inf-swipe-peek-left" id="inf8-peek-left"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;

      &lt;/div&gt;

        &lt;div class="inf-swipe-card" id="inf8-card-text"&gt;Created an original post or video&lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;div class="inf-freq-btns" id="inf8-freq-btns"&gt;
        &lt;button type="button" class="inf-freq-btn" data-col="c1" data-val="1"&gt;Never&lt;/button&gt;
        &lt;button type="button" class="inf-freq-btn" data-col="c2" data-val="2"&gt;Not in the&lt;br&gt;past 30 days&lt;/button&gt;
        &lt;button type="button" class="inf-freq-btn" data-col="c3" data-val="3"&gt;One time&lt;/button&gt;
        &lt;button type="button" class="inf-freq-btn" data-col="c4" data-val="4"&gt;2 - 4 times&lt;/button&gt;

      &lt;/div&gt;

        &lt;div class="inf-swipe-dot inf-active" data-idx="0"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

        &lt;div class="inf-swipe-dot" data-idx="2"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;

  &lt;/div&gt;

  &lt;div class="inf-continue-wrap" id="inf2-continue-wrap"&gt;
    &lt;button type="button" class="inf-continue-btn" id="inf2-continue" disabled&gt;CONTINUE &lt;span class="inf-arrow"&gt;&amp;#8250;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/button&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;

</style><style mode="after" name="question.footer">
&lt;script&gt;
(function(){
  /* Guard: only run on page.group.6 */
  if(!document.getElementById('inf2-root')) return;

  /* ---- find Decipher question element by label ---- */
  function findQ(q){
    var el = document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]');
    if(el &amp;&amp; el.closest &amp;&amp; !el.classList.contains('question')){
      var par = el.closest('.question');
      if(par) el = par;
    }
    return el;
  }

  /* ---- Debug init ---- */
  var allQ = document.querySelectorAll('.question');
  console.log('[INF2-page init] All .question IDs:', [].map.call(allQ, function(e){return e.id;}));
  ['INF2','INF3','INF4','INF5','INF6','INF7','INF8'].forEach(function(q){
    var el = findQ(q);
    if(el){
      var inputs = el.querySelectorAll('input');
      console.log('[INF2-page init] '+q+' found id='+el.id+' inputs='+inputs.length);
      [].forEach.call(inputs, function(inp){
        console.log('  type='+inp.type+' name='+inp.name+' value='+inp.value);
      });
    } else {
      console.log('[INF2-page init] '+q+' NOT in DOM (cond=false or missing)');
    }
  });

  /* ---- sync checkbox to native Decipher input ---- */
  function syncCheckbox(qLabel, rowLabel, checked){
    var box = findQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[syncCB] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;

    inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+qLabel+'_'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][value="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name$="_'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp){
      var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(m){
        var idx = parseInt(m[1], 10);
        var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
        if(idx === 99){
          for(var k=0; k&lt;allCB.length; k++){
            var nm = (allCB[k].name||'')+(allCB[k].className||'');
            if(nm.indexOf('noanswer')!==-1||nm.indexOf('exclusive')!==-1){inp=allCB[k]; break;}
          }
          if(!inp &amp;&amp; allCB.length&gt;0) inp = allCB[allCB.length-1];
        } else if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=allCB.length){
          inp = allCB[idx-1];
        }
      }
    }
    if(!inp){
      var all2 = box.querySelectorAll('input');
      for(var j=0; j&lt;all2.length; j++){
        if(all2[j].value===rowLabel||(all2[j].name&amp;&amp;all2[j].name.indexOf(rowLabel)!==-1)){inp=all2[j]; break;}
      }
    }

    if(inp){
      console.log('[syncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' checked='+checked+' (name='+inp.name+' val='+inp.value+')');
      if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[syncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' NO INPUT FOUND');
    }
  }

  /* ---- sync radio to native Decipher input ---- */
  function syncRadio(qLabel, val){
    var box = findQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[syncRadio] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    var inp = null;
    for(var i=0; i&lt;all.length; i++){
      if(all[i].value === val || all[i].value === 'r'+val){ inp = all[i]; break; }
    }
    if(!inp){
      var idx = parseInt(val,10);
      if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=all.length) inp = all[idx-1];
    }
    if(inp){
      console.log('[syncRadio] '+qLabel+' val='+val+' (name='+inp.name+' value='+inp.value+')');
      inp.checked = true;
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
    } else {
      console.warn('[syncRadio] '+qLabel+' val='+val+' NOT FOUND');
    }
  }

  /* ---- sync card-rating to native Decipher input ---- */
  function syncRating(qLabel, rowLabel, colVal){
    var box = findQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[syncRating] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    var inp = null;
    for(var i=0; i&lt;all.length; i++){
      var name = all[i].name || '';
      var v = all[i].value;
      if(name === qLabel+'_'+rowLabel &amp;&amp; (v === colVal || v === 'c'+colVal)){ inp = all[i]; break; }
    }
    if(!inp){
      /* Try: find row container, then radio by value */
      var rowEls = box.querySelectorAll('[class*="'+rowLabel+'"], [data-row="'+rowLabel+'"], tr[id*="'+rowLabel+'"]');
      for(var r=0; r&lt;rowEls.length &amp;&amp; !inp; r++){
        var radios = rowEls[r].querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
        for(var j=0; j&lt;radios.length; j++){
          if(radios[j].value === colVal || radios[j].value === 'c'+colVal){ inp = radios[j]; break; }
        }
      }
    }
    if(!inp){
      /* Position-based fallback: group radios by name, find row group, select by col index */
      var groups = {};
      for(var k=0; k&lt;all.length; k++){
        var n = all[k].name;
        if(!groups[n]) groups[n] = [];
        groups[n].push(all[k]);
      }
      var gKeys = Object.keys(groups);
      var rowMatch = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      var colMatch = colVal.match ? colVal.match(/^(\d+)$/) : null;
      if(rowMatch &amp;&amp; gKeys.length &gt;= parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)){
        var rowGroup = groups[gKeys[parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)-1]];
        var cIdx = colMatch ? parseInt(colMatch[1],10)-1 : parseInt(colVal,10)-1;
        if(rowGroup &amp;&amp; cIdx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; cIdx &lt; rowGroup.length){
          inp = rowGroup[cIdx];
        }
      }
    }

    if(inp){
      console.log('[syncRating] '+qLabel+' '+rowLabel+'='+colVal+' (name='+inp.name+' value='+inp.value+')');
      inp.checked = true;
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
    } else {
      console.warn('[syncRating] '+qLabel+' '+rowLabel+'='+colVal+' NOT FOUND');
    }
  }

  /* ==================================================================
     MERGED CHECKLIST + 3-CARD LAYOUT (no progressive disclosure)
     ================================================================== */

  var MERGED_LABELS = ['INF2','INF3','INF4','INF5'];
  var visibleCBs = [];
  MERGED_LABELS.forEach(function(q){
    if(findQ(q)){
      visibleCBs.push(q);
      console.log('[MERGED] '+q+' in DOM');
    } else {
      console.log('[MERGED] '+q+' NOT in DOM (cond=false)');
      document.querySelectorAll('#inf-merged-checks .inf-check-row[data-q="'+q+'"]').forEach(function(r){
        r.style.display = 'none';
      });
    }
  });

  /* INF6 is always visible (no condition) but track separately */
  var inf6Visible = !!findQ('INF6');

  /* Track 4 cards */
  var cardAnswered = { checklist: false, INF6: false, INF7: false, INF8: false };
  var hasAnyRows = document.querySelectorAll('#inf-merged-checks .inf-check-row:not([style*="display: none"])').length &gt; 0;
  if(!hasAnyRows) cardAnswered.checklist = true;
  if(!inf6Visible) cardAnswered.INF6 = true;

  function updateContinue(){
    var allDone = cardAnswered.checklist &amp;&amp; cardAnswered.INF6 &amp;&amp; cardAnswered.INF7 &amp;&amp; cardAnswered.INF8;
    document.getElementById('inf2-continue').disabled = !allDone;
  }

  /* ==================================================================
     MERGED CHECKLIST
     ================================================================== */
  var mergedSelected = {};
  var mergedNone = false;
  var noneBtn = document.getElementById('inf-merged-none');

  document.querySelectorAll('#inf-merged-checks .inf-check-row').forEach(function(row){
    if(row.style.display === 'none') return;
    row.addEventListener('click', function(){
      var q = row.getAttribute('data-q');
      var r = row.getAttribute('data-row');
      var key = q+'_'+r;
      mergedSelected[key] = !mergedSelected[key];
      row.classList.toggle('inf-checked', mergedSelected[key]);
      syncCheckbox(q, r, mergedSelected[key]);

      if(mergedSelected[key] &amp;&amp; mergedNone){
        mergedNone = false;
        if(noneBtn) noneBtn.classList.remove('inf-sel');
        visibleCBs.forEach(function(qq){ syncCheckbox(qq, 'r99', false); });
      }

      cardAnswered.checklist = mergedNone || Object.keys(mergedSelected).some(function(k){ return mergedSelected[k]; });
      updateContinue();
    });
  });

  if(noneBtn){
    noneBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      mergedNone = !mergedNone;
      noneBtn.classList.toggle('inf-sel', mergedNone);
      visibleCBs.forEach(function(q){ syncCheckbox(q, 'r99', mergedNone); });

      if(mergedNone){
        document.querySelectorAll('#inf-merged-checks .inf-check-row').forEach(function(row){
          if(row.style.display === 'none') return;
          var q2 = row.getAttribute('data-q');
          var r2 = row.getAttribute('data-row');
          mergedSelected[q2+'_'+r2] = false;
          row.classList.remove('inf-checked');
          syncCheckbox(q2, r2, false);
        });
      }

      cardAnswered.checklist = mergedNone || Object.keys(mergedSelected).some(function(k){ return mergedSelected[k]; });
      updateContinue();
    });
  }

  /* ==================================================================
     INF6 SEPARATE CARD
     ================================================================== */
  var inf6Selected = {};
  var inf6None = false;
  var inf6NoneBtn = document.getElementById('inf6-none');

  document.querySelectorAll('#inf6-checks .inf-check-row').forEach(function(row){
    row.addEventListener('click', function(){
      var r = row.getAttribute('data-row');
      inf6Selected[r] = !inf6Selected[r];
      row.classList.toggle('inf-checked', inf6Selected[r]);
      syncCheckbox('INF6', r, inf6Selected[r]);

      if(inf6Selected[r] &amp;&amp; inf6None){
        inf6None = false;
        if(inf6NoneBtn) inf6NoneBtn.classList.remove('inf-sel');
        syncCheckbox('INF6', 'r99', false);
      }

      cardAnswered.INF6 = inf6None || Object.keys(inf6Selected).some(function(k){ return inf6Selected[k]; });
      updateContinue();
    });
  });

  if(inf6NoneBtn){
    inf6NoneBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      inf6None = !inf6None;
      inf6NoneBtn.classList.toggle('inf-sel', inf6None);
      syncCheckbox('INF6', 'r99', inf6None);

      if(inf6None){
        document.querySelectorAll('#inf6-checks .inf-check-row').forEach(function(row){
          var r2 = row.getAttribute('data-row');
          inf6Selected[r2] = false;
          row.classList.remove('inf-checked');
          syncCheckbox('INF6', r2, false);
        });
      }

      cardAnswered.INF6 = inf6None || Object.keys(inf6Selected).some(function(k){ return inf6Selected[k]; });
      updateContinue();
    });
  }

  /* ==================================================================
     BUTTON-SELECT GRID (INF7)
     ================================================================== */

  var inf7Grid = document.querySelector('.inf-btn-grid[data-q="INF7"]');
  if(inf7Grid){
    inf7Grid.querySelectorAll('.inf-btn-option').forEach(function(opt){
      opt.addEventListener('click', function(){
        inf7Grid.querySelectorAll('.inf-btn-option').forEach(function(o){ o.classList.remove('inf-sel','inf-flash'); });
        opt.classList.add('inf-flash');
        var val = opt.getAttribute('data-val');
        syncRadio('INF7', val);
        cardAnswered.INF7 = true;
        updateContinue();
        setTimeout(function(){
          opt.classList.remove('inf-flash');
          opt.classList.add('inf-sel');
        }, 400);
      });
    });
  }

  /* ==================================================================
     CARD-SWIPE RATING (INF8)
     ================================================================== */

  var swipeItems = [
    {row: 'r1', text: 'Created an original post or video'},
    {row: 'r2', text: 'Shared or reposted content'},
    {row: 'r3', text: 'Commented or replied to posts'}
  ];
  var swipeIdx = 0;
  var swipeAnswers = {};
  var cardText = document.getElementById('inf8-card-text');
  var peekLeft = document.getElementById('inf8-peek-left');
  var peekRight = document.getElementById('inf8-peek-right');
  var freqBtns = document.getElementById('inf8-freq-btns');
  var dotsEl = document.getElementById('inf8-dots');

  function updateSwipe(){
    if(!cardText) return;
    cardText.textContent = swipeItems[swipeIdx].text;
    if(peekLeft) peekLeft.textContent = swipeIdx &gt; 0 ? swipeItems[swipeIdx-1].text : '';
    if(peekRight) peekRight.textContent = swipeIdx &lt; swipeItems.length-1 ? swipeItems[swipeIdx+1].text : '';
    if(freqBtns){
      var cur = swipeAnswers[swipeItems[swipeIdx].row];
      freqBtns.querySelectorAll('.inf-freq-btn').forEach(function(b){
        b.classList.remove('inf-flash');
        b.classList.toggle('inf-sel', b.getAttribute('data-col') === cur);
      });
    }
    if(dotsEl){
      dotsEl.querySelectorAll('.inf-swipe-dot').forEach(function(dot, i){
        dot.classList.toggle('inf-active', i === swipeIdx);
        dot.classList.toggle('inf-done', !!swipeAnswers[swipeItems[i].row]);
      });
    }
  }

  if(freqBtns){
    freqBtns.querySelectorAll('.inf-freq-btn').forEach(function(btn){
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var col = btn.getAttribute('data-col');
        var val = btn.getAttribute('data-val');
        swipeAnswers[swipeItems[swipeIdx].row] = col;
        syncRating('INF8', swipeItems[swipeIdx].row, val);
        var allRated = swipeItems.every(function(item){ return swipeAnswers[item.row]; });
        cardAnswered.INF8 = allRated;

        /* Green flash highlight then auto-advance */
        freqBtns.querySelectorAll('.inf-freq-btn').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('inf-sel','inf-flash'); });
        btn.classList.add('inf-flash');
        setTimeout(function(){
          btn.classList.remove('inf-flash');
          btn.classList.add('inf-sel');
          if(swipeIdx &lt; swipeItems.length - 1){
            setTimeout(function(){ swipeIdx++; updateSwipe(); }, 150);
          } else {
            updateSwipe();
          }
          updateContinue();
        }, 400);
      });
    });
  }

  updateSwipe();

  /* ==================================================================
     CONTINUE BUTTON
     ================================================================== */

  var continueBtn = document.getElementById('inf2-continue');
  if(continueBtn){
    continueBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(continueBtn.disabled) return;
      console.log('[INF2 SUBMIT] cardAnswered:', JSON.stringify(cardAnswered));

      /* Set r99 on visible checkbox questions with no selections */
      var allCBLabels = visibleCBs.concat(inf6Visible ? ['INF6'] : []);
      allCBLabels.forEach(function(q){
        var box = findQ(q);
        if(!box) return;
        var chkd = box.querySelectorAll('input:checked');
        if(chkd.length === 0){
          console.log('[SUBMIT] '+q+' no selections, auto-setting r99');
          syncCheckbox(q, 'r99', true);
        }
      });
      ['INF7','INF8'].forEach(function(q){
        var box = findQ(q);
        if(!box) return;
        var chkd = box.querySelectorAll('input:checked');
        console.log('[INF2 SUBMIT] '+q+' native checked: '+chkd.length);
        if(chkd.length === 0 &amp;&amp; cardAnswered[q]){
          console.warn('[INF2 SUBMIT] '+q+' FALLBACK: force-setting by position');
          var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
          if(allCB.length &gt; 0){
            if(noneStates[q]){
              var last = allCB[allCB.length-1];
              last.checked = true; last.click();
              try{ jQuery(last).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
            } else if(checkStates[q]){
              Object.keys(checkStates[q]).forEach(function(r){
                if(!checkStates[q][r]) return;
                var m3 = r.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
                if(m3){
                  var i3 = parseInt(m3[1],10)-1;
                  if(i3&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; i3&lt;allCB.length){
                    allCB[i3].checked = true; allCB[i3].click();
                    try{ jQuery(allCB[i3]).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
                  }
                }
              });
            }
          }
        }
      });

      var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
      if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
      if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
      } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
      }
    });
  }

  /* INIT */
  updateContinue();
})();

function nmFindQ(q){
    var el = document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]');
    if(el &amp;&amp; el.closest &amp;&amp; !el.classList.contains('question')){
      var par = el.closest('.question');
      if(par) el = par;
    }
    return el;
}
function nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, rowLabel, checked){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 0: cached lookup */
    if(window._nmCBCache &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel] &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel]){
      inp = window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel];
      if(inp){ if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click(); return; }
      inp = null;
    }
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][value="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name*="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.0.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      var prefix = '';
      for(var pi=0; pi&lt;allCB.length; pi++){
        var nm = allCB[pi].name || '';
        var ld = nm.lastIndexOf('.');
        if(ld &gt; 0){ prefix = nm.substring(0, ld+1); break; }
      }
      if(prefix){
        var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m){
          var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
          if(rNum === 99){
            var maxSfx = -1;
            for(var si=0; si&lt;allCB.length; si++){
              var sfx = parseInt((allCB[si].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
              if(sfx &gt; maxSfx) maxSfx = sfx;
            }
            if(maxSfx &gt;= 0) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+maxSfx+'"]');
          } else {
            inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+(rNum-1)+'"]');
          }
        }
      }
      /* Fallback: position-based (works when no shuffle) */
      if(!inp &amp;&amp; allCB.length &gt; 0){
        var m2 = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m2){
          var idx = parseInt(m2[1], 10);
          if(idx === 99){
            for(var ki=0; ki&lt;allCB.length; ki++){
              var nm2 = (allCB[ki].name||'')+(allCB[ki].className||'');
              if(nm2.indexOf('noanswer')!==-1||nm2.indexOf('exclusive')!==-1){inp=allCB[ki]; break;}
            }
            if(!inp) inp = allCB[allCB.length-1];
          } else if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=allCB.length){
            inp = allCB[idx-1];
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Cache and apply */
    if(inp){
      if(!window._nmCBCache) window._nmCBCache = {};
      if(!window._nmCBCache[qLabel]) window._nmCBCache[qLabel] = {};
      window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel] = inp;
      if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' NO INPUT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncRating(qLabel, rowLabel, colVal){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;all.length; i++){
      var name = all[i].name || '';
      var v = all[i].value;
      if(name.indexOf(rowLabel) !== -1 &amp;&amp; (v === colVal || v === 'c'+colVal)){ inp = all[i]; break; }
    }
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(m){
        var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
        var defIdx = (rNum === 99) ? -1 : rNum - 1;
        /* Try selects first */
        var allSel = box.querySelectorAll('select');
        if(allSel.length &gt; 0){
          var selPrefix = '';
          for(var si=0; si&lt;allSel.length; si++){
            var sn = allSel[si].name || '';
            var sld = sn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(sld &gt; 0){ selPrefix = sn.substring(0, sld+1); break; }
          }
          if(selPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxS = -1;
              for(var sk=0; sk&lt;allSel.length; sk++){
                var ss = parseInt((allSel[sk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(ss &gt; maxS) maxS = ss;
              }
              defIdx = maxS;
            }
            var sel = box.querySelector('select[name="'+selPrefix+defIdx+'"]');
            if(sel){
              sel.value = colVal;
              if(!sel.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel.value = 'c'+colVal;
              sel.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
              try{ jQuery(sel).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
              return;
            }
          }
        }
        /* Try radios by definition-index */
        if(!inp &amp;&amp; all.length &gt; 0){
          var rPrefix = '';
          for(var ri=0; ri&lt;all.length; ri++){
            var rn = all[ri].name || '';
            var rld = rn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(rld &gt; 0){ rPrefix = rn.substring(0, rld+1); break; }
          }
          if(rPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxR = -1;
              var rNames = {};
              for(var rk=0; rk&lt;all.length; rk++){
                var rs = parseInt((all[rk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(rs &gt; maxR) maxR = rs;
              }
              defIdx = maxR;
            }
            var targetName = rPrefix + defIdx;
            for(var rj=0; rj&lt;all.length; rj++){
              if(all[rj].name === targetName &amp;&amp; (all[rj].value === colVal || all[rj].value === 'c'+colVal)){
                inp = all[rj]; break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 3: position-based fallback (works when no shuffle) */
    if(!inp){
      var groups = {};
      for(var k=0; k&lt;all.length; k++){
        var n = all[k].name;
        if(!groups[n]) groups[n] = [];
        groups[n].push(all[k]);
      }
      var gKeys = Object.keys(groups);
      var rowMatch = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(rowMatch &amp;&amp; gKeys.length &gt;= parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)){
        var rowGroup = groups[gKeys[parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)-1]];
        var colMatch = colVal.match ? colVal.match(/^(\d+)$/) : null;
        var cIdx = colMatch ? parseInt(colMatch[1],10)-1 : parseInt(colVal,10)-1;
        if(rowGroup &amp;&amp; cIdx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; cIdx &lt; rowGroup.length){
          inp = rowGroup[cIdx];
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 4: select by name pattern */
    if(!inp){
      var sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name="'+qLabel+'_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(!sel2) sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name*="_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(sel2){
        sel2.value = colVal;
        if(!sel2.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel2.value = 'c'+colVal;
        sel2.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
        try{ jQuery(sel2).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
        return;
      }
    }
    if(inp){
      inp.checked = true;
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' '+rowLabel+'='+colVal+' NOT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncText(qLabel, val){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return;
    var inp = q.querySelector('textarea') || q.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
    if(inp){
        inp.value = val;
        try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('change').trigger('input'); }catch(e){}
    }
}
function nmClickNext(){
    var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
    if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
    } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
    }
}
function nmGetRows(qLabel){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return [];
    var rows = [], seen = {};
    var inputs = q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"], input[type="checkbox"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;inputs.length; i++){
        var inp = inputs[i];
        var name = inp.name || '';
        var m = name.match(new RegExp('^'+qLabel+'_(r\\d+)'));
        if(!m) continue;
        var rLabel = m[1];
        if(seen[rLabel] || rLabel === 'r99') continue;
        seen[rLabel] = true;
        var rowEl = inp.closest('.fir-row') || inp.closest('tr') || inp.closest('.row-elements');
        if(!rowEl) rowEl = inp.parentNode;
        var textEl = rowEl ? (rowEl.querySelector('.fir-text') || rowEl.querySelector('.row-text') || rowEl.querySelector('label')) : null;
        var txt = textEl ? textEl.textContent.trim() : rLabel;
        if(txt === rLabel || txt.length &lt; 2){
            var parent = inp.closest('.fir-row');
            if(parent){
                var fc = parent.querySelector('.fir-text-container, .fir-text, td:first-child, .row-label');
                if(fc) txt = fc.textContent.trim();
            }
        }
        rows.push({r: rLabel, name: txt});
    }
    return rows;
}

(function(){
  /* Progress bar: page 1 of 3 = 33% */
  var pf = document.getElementById('nm-progress-fill');
  if(pf) pf.style.width = '33%';

  var qLabel = 'NM_PLAT';
  var checks = {};
  var noneActive = false;
  var list = document.getElementById('nm-plat-list');
  var noneBtn = document.getElementById('nm-plat-none');
  var continueBtn = document.getElementById('nm-continue');
  function updateContinue(){
    var any = noneActive || Object.keys(checks).some(function(k){ return checks[k]; });
    continueBtn.disabled = !any;
  }
  if(list){
    list.querySelectorAll('.nm-check-row').forEach(function(row){
      row.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var r = row.getAttribute('data-row');
        checks[r] = !checks[r];
        row.classList.toggle('nm-checked', checks[r]);
        nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, r, checks[r]);
        if(checks[r] &amp;&amp; noneActive){
          noneActive = false;
          noneBtn.classList.remove('nm-sel');
          nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, 'r99', false);
        }
        updateContinue();
      });
    });
  }
  if(noneBtn){
    noneBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      noneActive = !noneActive;
      noneBtn.classList.toggle('nm-sel', noneActive);
      nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, 'r99', noneActive);
      if(noneActive){
        Object.keys(checks).forEach(function(r){ checks[r] = false; });
        list.querySelectorAll('.nm-check-row').forEach(function(row){ row.classList.remove('nm-checked'); });
        var q = nmFindQ(qLabel);
        if(q) q.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(function(cb){
          if(cb.name &amp;&amp; cb.name.indexOf('r99') === -1 &amp;&amp; cb.checked){ cb.click(); }
        });
      }
      updateContinue();
    });
  }
  if(continueBtn){
    continueBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(continueBtn.disabled) return;
      nmClickNext();
    });
  }
  updateContinue();
})();
