function nmFindQ(q){
    var el = document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]');
    if(el &amp;&amp; el.closest &amp;&amp; !el.classList.contains('question')){
      var par = el.closest('.question');
      if(par) el = par;
    }
    return el;
}
function nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, rowLabel, checked){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 0: cached lookup */
    if(window._nmCBCache &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel] &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel]){
      inp = window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel];
      if(inp){ if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click(); return; }
      inp = null;
    }
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][value="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name*="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.0.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      var prefix = '';
      for(var pi=0; pi&lt;allCB.length; pi++){
        var nm = allCB[pi].name || '';
        var ld = nm.lastIndexOf('.');
        if(ld &gt; 0){ prefix = nm.substring(0, ld+1); break; }
      }
      if(prefix){
        var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m){
          var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
          if(rNum === 99){
            var maxSfx = -1;
            for(var si=0; si&lt;allCB.length; si++){
              var sfx = parseInt((allCB[si].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
              if(sfx &gt; maxSfx) maxSfx = sfx;
            }
            if(maxSfx &gt;= 0) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+maxSfx+'"]');
          } else {
            inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+(rNum-1)+'"]');
          }
        }
      }
      /* Fallback: position-based (works when no shuffle) */
      if(!inp &amp;&amp; allCB.length &gt; 0){
        var m2 = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m2){
          var idx = parseInt(m2[1], 10);
          if(idx === 99){
            for(var ki=0; ki&lt;allCB.length; ki++){
              var nm2 = (allCB[ki].name||'')+(allCB[ki].className||'');
              if(nm2.indexOf('noanswer')!==-1||nm2.indexOf('exclusive')!==-1){inp=allCB[ki]; break;}
            }
            if(!inp) inp = allCB[allCB.length-1];
          } else if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=allCB.length){
            inp = allCB[idx-1];
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Cache and apply */
    if(inp){
      if(!window._nmCBCache) window._nmCBCache = {};
      if(!window._nmCBCache[qLabel]) window._nmCBCache[qLabel] = {};
      window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel] = inp;
      if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' NO INPUT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncRating(qLabel, rowLabel, colVal){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;all.length; i++){
      var name = all[i].name || '';
      var v = all[i].value;
      if(name.indexOf(rowLabel) !== -1 &amp;&amp; (v === colVal || v === 'c'+colVal)){ inp = all[i]; break; }
    }
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(m){
        var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
        var defIdx = (rNum === 99) ? -1 : rNum - 1;
        /* Try selects first */
        var allSel = box.querySelectorAll('select');
        if(allSel.length &gt; 0){
          var selPrefix = '';
          for(var si=0; si&lt;allSel.length; si++){
            var sn = allSel[si].name || '';
            var sld = sn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(sld &gt; 0){ selPrefix = sn.substring(0, sld+1); break; }
          }
          if(selPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxS = -1;
              for(var sk=0; sk&lt;allSel.length; sk++){
                var ss = parseInt((allSel[sk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(ss &gt; maxS) maxS = ss;
              }
              defIdx = maxS;
            }
            var sel = box.querySelector('select[name="'+selPrefix+defIdx+'"]');
            if(sel){
              sel.value = colVal;
              if(!sel.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel.value = 'c'+colVal;
              sel.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
              try{ jQuery(sel).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
              return;
            }
          }
        }
        /* Try radios by definition-index */
        if(!inp &amp;&amp; all.length &gt; 0){
          var rPrefix = '';
          for(var ri=0; ri&lt;all.length; ri++){
            var rn = all[ri].name || '';
            var rld = rn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(rld &gt; 0){ rPrefix = rn.substring(0, rld+1); break; }
          }
          if(rPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxR = -1;
              var rNames = {};
              for(var rk=0; rk&lt;all.length; rk++){
                var rs = parseInt((all[rk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(rs &gt; maxR) maxR = rs;
              }
              defIdx = maxR;
            }
            var targetName = rPrefix + defIdx;
            for(var rj=0; rj&lt;all.length; rj++){
              if(all[rj].name === targetName &amp;&amp; (all[rj].value === colVal || all[rj].value === 'c'+colVal)){
                inp = all[rj]; break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 3: position-based fallback (works when no shuffle) */
    if(!inp){
      var groups = {};
      for(var k=0; k&lt;all.length; k++){
        var n = all[k].name;
        if(!groups[n]) groups[n] = [];
        groups[n].push(all[k]);
      }
      var gKeys = Object.keys(groups);
      var rowMatch = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(rowMatch &amp;&amp; gKeys.length &gt;= parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)){
        var rowGroup = groups[gKeys[parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)-1]];
        var colMatch = colVal.match ? colVal.match(/^(\d+)$/) : null;
        var cIdx = colMatch ? parseInt(colMatch[1],10)-1 : parseInt(colVal,10)-1;
        if(rowGroup &amp;&amp; cIdx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; cIdx &lt; rowGroup.length){
          inp = rowGroup[cIdx];
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 4: select by name pattern */
    if(!inp){
      var sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name="'+qLabel+'_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(!sel2) sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name*="_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(sel2){
        sel2.value = colVal;
        if(!sel2.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel2.value = 'c'+colVal;
        sel2.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
        try{ jQuery(sel2).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
        return;
      }
    }
    if(inp){
      inp.checked = true;
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' '+rowLabel+'='+colVal+' NOT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncText(qLabel, val){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return;
    var inp = q.querySelector('textarea') || q.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
    if(inp){
        inp.value = val;
        try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('change').trigger('input'); }catch(e){}
    }
}
function nmClickNext(){
    var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
    if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
    } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
    }
}
function nmGetRows(qLabel){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return [];
    var rows = [], seen = {};
    var inputs = q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"], input[type="checkbox"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;inputs.length; i++){
        var inp = inputs[i];
        var name = inp.name || '';
        var m = name.match(new RegExp('^'+qLabel+'_(r\\d+)'));
        if(!m) continue;
        var rLabel = m[1];
        if(seen[rLabel] || rLabel === 'r99') continue;
        seen[rLabel] = true;
        var rowEl = inp.closest('.fir-row') || inp.closest('tr') || inp.closest('.row-elements');
        if(!rowEl) rowEl = inp.parentNode;
        var textEl = rowEl ? (rowEl.querySelector('.fir-text') || rowEl.querySelector('.row-text') || rowEl.querySelector('label')) : null;
        var txt = textEl ? textEl.textContent.trim() : rLabel;
        if(txt === rLabel || txt.length &lt; 2){
            var parent = inp.closest('.fir-row');
            if(parent){
                var fc = parent.querySelector('.fir-text-container, .fir-text, td:first-child, .row-label');
                if(fc) txt = fc.textContent.trim();
            }
        }
        rows.push({r: rLabel, name: txt});
    }
    return rows;
}

function nmFindQ(q){
    var el = document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]');
    if(el &amp;&amp; el.closest &amp;&amp; !el.classList.contains('question')){
      var par = el.closest('.question');
      if(par) el = par;
    }
    return el;
}
function nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, rowLabel, checked){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 0: cached lookup */
    if(window._nmCBCache &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel] &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel]){
      inp = window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel];
      if(inp){ if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click(); return; }
      inp = null;
    }
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][value="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name*="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.0.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      var prefix = '';
      for(var pi=0; pi&lt;allCB.length; pi++){
        var nm = allCB[pi].name || '';
        var ld = nm.lastIndexOf('.');
        if(ld &gt; 0){ prefix = nm.substring(0, ld+1); break; }
      }
      if(prefix){
        var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m){
          var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
          if(rNum === 99){
            var maxSfx = -1;
            for(var si=0; si&lt;allCB.length; si++){
              var sfx = parseInt((allCB[si].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
              if(sfx &gt; maxSfx) maxSfx = sfx;
            }
            if(maxSfx &gt;= 0) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+maxSfx+'"]');
          } else {
            inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+(rNum-1)+'"]');
          }
        }
      }
      /* Fallback: position-based (works when no shuffle) */
      if(!inp &amp;&amp; allCB.length &gt; 0){
        var m2 = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m2){
          var idx = parseInt(m2[1], 10);
          if(idx === 99){
            for(var ki=0; ki&lt;allCB.length; ki++){
              var nm2 = (allCB[ki].name||'')+(allCB[ki].className||'');
              if(nm2.indexOf('noanswer')!==-1||nm2.indexOf('exclusive')!==-1){inp=allCB[ki]; break;}
            }
            if(!inp) inp = allCB[allCB.length-1];
          } else if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=allCB.length){
            inp = allCB[idx-1];
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Cache and apply */
    if(inp){
      if(!window._nmCBCache) window._nmCBCache = {};
      if(!window._nmCBCache[qLabel]) window._nmCBCache[qLabel] = {};
      window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel] = inp;
      if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' NO INPUT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncRating(qLabel, rowLabel, colVal){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;all.length; i++){
      var name = all[i].name || '';
      var v = all[i].value;
      if(name.indexOf(rowLabel) !== -1 &amp;&amp; (v === colVal || v === 'c'+colVal)){ inp = all[i]; break; }
    }
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(m){
        var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
        var defIdx = (rNum === 99) ? -1 : rNum - 1;
        /* Try selects first */
        var allSel = box.querySelectorAll('select');
        if(allSel.length &gt; 0){
          var selPrefix = '';
          for(var si=0; si&lt;allSel.length; si++){
            var sn = allSel[si].name || '';
            var sld = sn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(sld &gt; 0){ selPrefix = sn.substring(0, sld+1); break; }
          }
          if(selPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxS = -1;
              for(var sk=0; sk&lt;allSel.length; sk++){
                var ss = parseInt((allSel[sk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(ss &gt; maxS) maxS = ss;
              }
              defIdx = maxS;
            }
            var sel = box.querySelector('select[name="'+selPrefix+defIdx+'"]');
            if(sel){
              sel.value = colVal;
              if(!sel.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel.value = 'c'+colVal;
              sel.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
              try{ jQuery(sel).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
              return;
            }
          }
        }
        /* Try radios by definition-index */
        if(!inp &amp;&amp; all.length &gt; 0){
          var rPrefix = '';
          for(var ri=0; ri&lt;all.length; ri++){
            var rn = all[ri].name || '';
            var rld = rn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(rld &gt; 0){ rPrefix = rn.substring(0, rld+1); break; }
          }
          if(rPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxR = -1;
              var rNames = {};
              for(var rk=0; rk&lt;all.length; rk++){
                var rs = parseInt((all[rk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(rs &gt; maxR) maxR = rs;
              }
              defIdx = maxR;
            }
            var targetName = rPrefix + defIdx;
            for(var rj=0; rj&lt;all.length; rj++){
              if(all[rj].name === targetName &amp;&amp; (all[rj].value === colVal || all[rj].value === 'c'+colVal)){
                inp = all[rj]; break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 3: position-based fallback (works when no shuffle) */
    if(!inp){
      var groups = {};
      for(var k=0; k&lt;all.length; k++){
        var n = all[k].name;
        if(!groups[n]) groups[n] = [];
        groups[n].push(all[k]);
      }
      var gKeys = Object.keys(groups);
      var rowMatch = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(rowMatch &amp;&amp; gKeys.length &gt;= parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)){
        var rowGroup = groups[gKeys[parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)-1]];
        var colMatch = colVal.match ? colVal.match(/^(\d+)$/) : null;
        var cIdx = colMatch ? parseInt(colMatch[1],10)-1 : parseInt(colVal,10)-1;
        if(rowGroup &amp;&amp; cIdx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; cIdx &lt; rowGroup.length){
          inp = rowGroup[cIdx];
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 4: select by name pattern */
    if(!inp){
      var sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name="'+qLabel+'_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(!sel2) sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name*="_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(sel2){
        sel2.value = colVal;
        if(!sel2.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel2.value = 'c'+colVal;
        sel2.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
        try{ jQuery(sel2).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
        return;
      }
    }
    if(inp){
      inp.checked = true;
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' '+rowLabel+'='+colVal+' NOT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncText(qLabel, val){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return;
    var inp = q.querySelector('textarea') || q.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
    if(inp){
        inp.value = val;
        try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('change').trigger('input'); }catch(e){}
    }
}
function nmClickNext(){
    var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
    if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
    } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
    }
}
function nmGetRows(qLabel){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return [];
    var rows = [], seen = {};
    var inputs = q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"], input[type="checkbox"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;inputs.length; i++){
        var inp = inputs[i];
        var name = inp.name || '';
        var m = name.match(new RegExp('^'+qLabel+'_(r\\d+)'));
        if(!m) continue;
        var rLabel = m[1];
        if(seen[rLabel] || rLabel === 'r99') continue;
        seen[rLabel] = true;
        var rowEl = inp.closest('.fir-row') || inp.closest('tr') || inp.closest('.row-elements');
        if(!rowEl) rowEl = inp.parentNode;
        var textEl = rowEl ? (rowEl.querySelector('.fir-text') || rowEl.querySelector('.row-text') || rowEl.querySelector('label')) : null;
        var txt = textEl ? textEl.textContent.trim() : rLabel;
        if(txt === rLabel || txt.length &lt; 2){
            var parent = inp.closest('.fir-row');
            if(parent){
                var fc = parent.querySelector('.fir-text-container, .fir-text, td:first-child, .row-label');
                if(fc) txt = fc.textContent.trim();
            }
        }
        rows.push({r: rLabel, name: txt});
    }
    return rows;
}

function nmFindQ(q){
    var el = document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]');
    if(el &amp;&amp; el.closest &amp;&amp; !el.classList.contains('question')){
      var par = el.closest('.question');
      if(par) el = par;
    }
    return el;
}
function nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, rowLabel, checked){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 0: cached lookup */
    if(window._nmCBCache &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel] &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel]){
      inp = window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel];
      if(inp){ if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click(); return; }
      inp = null;
    }
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][value="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name*="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.0.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      var prefix = '';
      for(var pi=0; pi&lt;allCB.length; pi++){
        var nm = allCB[pi].name || '';
        var ld = nm.lastIndexOf('.');
        if(ld &gt; 0){ prefix = nm.substring(0, ld+1); break; }
      }
      if(prefix){
        var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m){
          var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
          if(rNum === 99){
            var maxSfx = -1;
            for(var si=0; si&lt;allCB.length; si++){
              var sfx = parseInt((allCB[si].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
              if(sfx &gt; maxSfx) maxSfx = sfx;
            }
            if(maxSfx &gt;= 0) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+maxSfx+'"]');
          } else {
            inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+(rNum-1)+'"]');
          }
        }
      }
      /* Fallback: position-based (works when no shuffle) */
      if(!inp &amp;&amp; allCB.length &gt; 0){
        var m2 = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m2){
          var idx = parseInt(m2[1], 10);
          if(idx === 99){
            for(var ki=0; ki&lt;allCB.length; ki++){
              var nm2 = (allCB[ki].name||'')+(allCB[ki].className||'');
              if(nm2.indexOf('noanswer')!==-1||nm2.indexOf('exclusive')!==-1){inp=allCB[ki]; break;}
            }
            if(!inp) inp = allCB[allCB.length-1];
          } else if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=allCB.length){
            inp = allCB[idx-1];
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Cache and apply */
    if(inp){
      if(!window._nmCBCache) window._nmCBCache = {};
      if(!window._nmCBCache[qLabel]) window._nmCBCache[qLabel] = {};
      window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel] = inp;
      if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' NO INPUT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncRating(qLabel, rowLabel, colVal){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;all.length; i++){
      var name = all[i].name || '';
      var v = all[i].value;
      if(name.indexOf(rowLabel) !== -1 &amp;&amp; (v === colVal || v === 'c'+colVal)){ inp = all[i]; break; }
    }
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(m){
        var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
        var defIdx = (rNum === 99) ? -1 : rNum - 1;
        /* Try selects first */
        var allSel = box.querySelectorAll('select');
        if(allSel.length &gt; 0){
          var selPrefix = '';
          for(var si=0; si&lt;allSel.length; si++){
            var sn = allSel[si].name || '';
            var sld = sn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(sld &gt; 0){ selPrefix = sn.substring(0, sld+1); break; }
          }
          if(selPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxS = -1;
              for(var sk=0; sk&lt;allSel.length; sk++){
                var ss = parseInt((allSel[sk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(ss &gt; maxS) maxS = ss;
              }
              defIdx = maxS;
            }
            var sel = box.querySelector('select[name="'+selPrefix+defIdx+'"]');
            if(sel){
              sel.value = colVal;
              if(!sel.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel.value = 'c'+colVal;
              sel.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
              try{ jQuery(sel).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
              return;
            }
          }
        }
        /* Try radios by definition-index */
        if(!inp &amp;&amp; all.length &gt; 0){
          var rPrefix = '';
          for(var ri=0; ri&lt;all.length; ri++){
            var rn = all[ri].name || '';
            var rld = rn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(rld &gt; 0){ rPrefix = rn.substring(0, rld+1); break; }
          }
          if(rPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxR = -1;
              var rNames = {};
              for(var rk=0; rk&lt;all.length; rk++){
                var rs = parseInt((all[rk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(rs &gt; maxR) maxR = rs;
              }
              defIdx = maxR;
            }
            var targetName = rPrefix + defIdx;
            for(var rj=0; rj&lt;all.length; rj++){
              if(all[rj].name === targetName &amp;&amp; (all[rj].value === colVal || all[rj].value === 'c'+colVal)){
                inp = all[rj]; break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 3: position-based fallback (works when no shuffle) */
    if(!inp){
      var groups = {};
      for(var k=0; k&lt;all.length; k++){
        var n = all[k].name;
        if(!groups[n]) groups[n] = [];
        groups[n].push(all[k]);
      }
      var gKeys = Object.keys(groups);
      var rowMatch = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(rowMatch &amp;&amp; gKeys.length &gt;= parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)){
        var rowGroup = groups[gKeys[parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)-1]];
        var colMatch = colVal.match ? colVal.match(/^(\d+)$/) : null;
        var cIdx = colMatch ? parseInt(colMatch[1],10)-1 : parseInt(colVal,10)-1;
        if(rowGroup &amp;&amp; cIdx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; cIdx &lt; rowGroup.length){
          inp = rowGroup[cIdx];
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 4: select by name pattern */
    if(!inp){
      var sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name="'+qLabel+'_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(!sel2) sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name*="_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(sel2){
        sel2.value = colVal;
        if(!sel2.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel2.value = 'c'+colVal;
        sel2.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
        try{ jQuery(sel2).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
        return;
      }
    }
    if(inp){
      inp.checked = true;
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' '+rowLabel+'='+colVal+' NOT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncText(qLabel, val){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return;
    var inp = q.querySelector('textarea') || q.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
    if(inp){
        inp.value = val;
        try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('change').trigger('input'); }catch(e){}
    }
}
function nmClickNext(){
    var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
    if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
    } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
    }
}
function nmGetRows(qLabel){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return [];
    var rows = [], seen = {};
    var inputs = q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"], input[type="checkbox"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;inputs.length; i++){
        var inp = inputs[i];
        var name = inp.name || '';
        var m = name.match(new RegExp('^'+qLabel+'_(r\\d+)'));
        if(!m) continue;
        var rLabel = m[1];
        if(seen[rLabel] || rLabel === 'r99') continue;
        seen[rLabel] = true;
        var rowEl = inp.closest('.fir-row') || inp.closest('tr') || inp.closest('.row-elements');
        if(!rowEl) rowEl = inp.parentNode;
        var textEl = rowEl ? (rowEl.querySelector('.fir-text') || rowEl.querySelector('.row-text') || rowEl.querySelector('label')) : null;
        var txt = textEl ? textEl.textContent.trim() : rLabel;
        if(txt === rLabel || txt.length &lt; 2){
            var parent = inp.closest('.fir-row');
            if(parent){
                var fc = parent.querySelector('.fir-text-container, .fir-text, td:first-child, .row-label');
                if(fc) txt = fc.textContent.trim();
            }
        }
        rows.push({r: rLabel, name: txt});
    }
    return rows;
}

  var qLabel = 'NM_SRC_T8';
  var oeLabel = 'NM_SRC_T8_OE';

  if(items.length === 0){console.warn('[nmFilter] '+qLabel+' EMPTY after filter, skipping'); return;}
  for(var _i=items.length-1;_i&gt;0;_i--){var _j=Math.floor(Math.random()*(_i+1));var _t=items[_i];items[_i]=items[_j];items[_j]=_t;}
  if(items.length&gt;25)items.length=25;
  var swipeIdx = 0, swipeAnswers = {}, oeNotSure = false;

  var counterEl = document.getElementById('nm-swipe-counter');

  var oeNotsure = document.getElementById('nm-oe-notsure');
  var continueBtn = document.getElementById('nm-continue');
  if(dotsEl){
    var dh = '';
    for(var i=0;i&lt;items.length;i++) dh += '&lt;div class="nm-swipe-dot'+(i===0?' nm-active':'')+'" data-idx="'+i+'"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
    dotsEl.innerHTML = dh;
  }
  function updateSwipe(){
    if(!cardText) return;
    cardText.textContent = items[swipeIdx].name;
    if(counterEl) counterEl.textContent = (swipeIdx+1)+' of '+items.length;
    if(freqBtns){
      var cur = swipeAnswers[items[swipeIdx].r];
      freqBtns.querySelectorAll('.nm-freq-btn-v2').forEach(function(b){
        b.classList.remove('nm-flash');
        b.classList.toggle('nm-sel', b.getAttribute('data-col') === cur);
      });
    }
    if(dotsEl){
      dotsEl.querySelectorAll('.nm-swipe-dot').forEach(function(dot, i){
        dot.classList.toggle('nm-active', i === swipeIdx);
        dot.classList.toggle('nm-done', !!swipeAnswers[items[i].r]);
      });
    }
  }
  function updateContinue(){
    var allRated = items.every(function(item){ return swipeAnswers[item.r]; });
    continueBtn.disabled = !allRated;
    if(allRated &amp;&amp; oeWrap) oeWrap.style.display = '';
  }
  if(freqBtns){
    freqBtns.querySelectorAll('.nm-freq-btn-v2').forEach(function(btn){
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var col = btn.getAttribute('data-col');
        var val = btn.getAttribute('data-val');
        swipeAnswers[items[swipeIdx].r] = col;
        nmSyncRating(qLabel, items[swipeIdx].r, val);
        freqBtns.querySelectorAll('.nm-freq-btn-v2').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('nm-sel','nm-flash'); });
        btn.classList.add('nm-flash');
        setTimeout(function(){
          btn.classList.remove('nm-flash');
          btn.classList.add('nm-sel');
          if(swipeIdx &lt; items.length - 1){
            setTimeout(function(){ swipeIdx++; updateSwipe(); }, 150);
          } else {
            updateSwipe();
          }
          updateContinue();
        }, 400);
      });
    });
  }
  if(oeInput){
    oeInput.addEventListener('input', function(){
      nmSyncText(oeLabel, oeInput.value);
      if(oeInput.value.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; oeNotSure){ oeNotSure = false; oeNotsure.classList.remove('nm-sel'); }
    });
  }
  if(oeNotsure){

      oeNotSure = !oeNotSure;
      oeNotsure.classList.toggle('nm-sel', oeNotSure);
      if(oeNotSure){ oeInput.value = 'Not Sure'; nmSyncText(oeLabel, 'Not Sure'); }
      else { oeInput.value = ''; nmSyncText(oeLabel, ''); }
    });
  }
  if(dotsEl){
    dotsEl.querySelectorAll('.nm-swipe-dot').forEach(function(dot){
      dot.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var idx = parseInt(dot.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
        if(!isNaN(idx) &amp;&amp; idx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; idx &lt; items.length){ swipeIdx = idx; updateSwipe(); }
      });
    });
  }
  if(continueBtn){
    continueBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(continueBtn.disabled) return;
      nmClickNext();
    });
  }
  updateSwipe();
  updateContinue();
})();

function nmFindQ(q){
    var el = document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]');
    if(el &amp;&amp; el.closest &amp;&amp; !el.classList.contains('question')){
      var par = el.closest('.question');
      if(par) el = par;
    }
    return el;
}
function nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, rowLabel, checked){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 0: cached lookup */
    if(window._nmCBCache &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel] &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel]){
      inp = window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel];
      if(inp){ if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click(); return; }
      inp = null;
    }
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][value="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name*="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.0.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      var prefix = '';
      for(var pi=0; pi&lt;allCB.length; pi++){
        var nm = allCB[pi].name || '';
        var ld = nm.lastIndexOf('.');
        if(ld &gt; 0){ prefix = nm.substring(0, ld+1); break; }
      }
      if(prefix){
        var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m){
          var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
          if(rNum === 99){
            var maxSfx = -1;
            for(var si=0; si&lt;allCB.length; si++){
              var sfx = parseInt((allCB[si].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
              if(sfx &gt; maxSfx) maxSfx = sfx;
            }
            if(maxSfx &gt;= 0) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+maxSfx+'"]');
          } else {
            inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+(rNum-1)+'"]');
          }
        }
      }
      /* Fallback: position-based (works when no shuffle) */
      if(!inp &amp;&amp; allCB.length &gt; 0){
        var m2 = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m2){
          var idx = parseInt(m2[1], 10);
          if(idx === 99){
            for(var ki=0; ki&lt;allCB.length; ki++){
              var nm2 = (allCB[ki].name||'')+(allCB[ki].className||'');
              if(nm2.indexOf('noanswer')!==-1||nm2.indexOf('exclusive')!==-1){inp=allCB[ki]; break;}
            }
            if(!inp) inp = allCB[allCB.length-1];
          } else if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=allCB.length){
            inp = allCB[idx-1];
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Cache and apply */
    if(inp){
      if(!window._nmCBCache) window._nmCBCache = {};
      if(!window._nmCBCache[qLabel]) window._nmCBCache[qLabel] = {};
      window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel] = inp;
      if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' NO INPUT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncRating(qLabel, rowLabel, colVal){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;all.length; i++){
      var name = all[i].name || '';
      var v = all[i].value;
      if(name.indexOf(rowLabel) !== -1 &amp;&amp; (v === colVal || v === 'c'+colVal)){ inp = all[i]; break; }
    }
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(m){
        var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
        var defIdx = (rNum === 99) ? -1 : rNum - 1;
        /* Try selects first */
        var allSel = box.querySelectorAll('select');
        if(allSel.length &gt; 0){
          var selPrefix = '';
          for(var si=0; si&lt;allSel.length; si++){
            var sn = allSel[si].name || '';
            var sld = sn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(sld &gt; 0){ selPrefix = sn.substring(0, sld+1); break; }
          }
          if(selPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxS = -1;
              for(var sk=0; sk&lt;allSel.length; sk++){
                var ss = parseInt((allSel[sk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(ss &gt; maxS) maxS = ss;
              }
              defIdx = maxS;
            }
            var sel = box.querySelector('select[name="'+selPrefix+defIdx+'"]');
            if(sel){
              sel.value = colVal;
              if(!sel.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel.value = 'c'+colVal;
              sel.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
              try{ jQuery(sel).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
              return;
            }
          }
        }
        /* Try radios by definition-index */
        if(!inp &amp;&amp; all.length &gt; 0){
          var rPrefix = '';
          for(var ri=0; ri&lt;all.length; ri++){
            var rn = all[ri].name || '';
            var rld = rn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(rld &gt; 0){ rPrefix = rn.substring(0, rld+1); break; }
          }
          if(rPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxR = -1;
              var rNames = {};
              for(var rk=0; rk&lt;all.length; rk++){
                var rs = parseInt((all[rk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(rs &gt; maxR) maxR = rs;
              }
              defIdx = maxR;
            }
            var targetName = rPrefix + defIdx;
            for(var rj=0; rj&lt;all.length; rj++){
              if(all[rj].name === targetName &amp;&amp; (all[rj].value === colVal || all[rj].value === 'c'+colVal)){
                inp = all[rj]; break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 3: position-based fallback (works when no shuffle) */
    if(!inp){
      var groups = {};
      for(var k=0; k&lt;all.length; k++){
        var n = all[k].name;
        if(!groups[n]) groups[n] = [];
        groups[n].push(all[k]);
      }
      var gKeys = Object.keys(groups);
      var rowMatch = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(rowMatch &amp;&amp; gKeys.length &gt;= parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)){
        var rowGroup = groups[gKeys[parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)-1]];
        var colMatch = colVal.match ? colVal.match(/^(\d+)$/) : null;
        var cIdx = colMatch ? parseInt(colMatch[1],10)-1 : parseInt(colVal,10)-1;
        if(rowGroup &amp;&amp; cIdx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; cIdx &lt; rowGroup.length){
          inp = rowGroup[cIdx];
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 4: select by name pattern */
    if(!inp){
      var sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name="'+qLabel+'_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(!sel2) sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name*="_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(sel2){
        sel2.value = colVal;
        if(!sel2.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel2.value = 'c'+colVal;
        sel2.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
        try{ jQuery(sel2).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
        return;
      }
    }
    if(inp){
      inp.checked = true;
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' '+rowLabel+'='+colVal+' NOT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncText(qLabel, val){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return;
    var inp = q.querySelector('textarea') || q.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
    if(inp){
        inp.value = val;
        try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('change').trigger('input'); }catch(e){}
    }
}
function nmClickNext(){
    var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
    if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
    } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
    }
}
function nmGetRows(qLabel){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return [];
    var rows = [], seen = {};
    var inputs = q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"], input[type="checkbox"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;inputs.length; i++){
        var inp = inputs[i];
        var name = inp.name || '';
        var m = name.match(new RegExp('^'+qLabel+'_(r\\d+)'));
        if(!m) continue;
        var rLabel = m[1];
        if(seen[rLabel] || rLabel === 'r99') continue;
        seen[rLabel] = true;
        var rowEl = inp.closest('.fir-row') || inp.closest('tr') || inp.closest('.row-elements');
        if(!rowEl) rowEl = inp.parentNode;
        var textEl = rowEl ? (rowEl.querySelector('.fir-text') || rowEl.querySelector('.row-text') || rowEl.querySelector('label')) : null;
        var txt = textEl ? textEl.textContent.trim() : rLabel;
        if(txt === rLabel || txt.length &lt; 2){
            var parent = inp.closest('.fir-row');
            if(parent){
                var fc = parent.querySelector('.fir-text-container, .fir-text, td:first-child, .row-label');
                if(fc) txt = fc.textContent.trim();
            }
        }
        rows.push({r: rLabel, name: txt});
    }
    return rows;
}

(function(){
  var qLabel = 'NM_INF_T8';
  var oeLabel = 'NM_INF_T8_OE';
  var items = [
    {r:'r1', name:'Mark Bell\'s Power Project'},
    {r:'r2', name:'Ben Greenfield Life'},
    {r:'r3', name:'Jocko Podcast'},
    {r:'r4', name:'Mike Israetel  (Renaissance Periodization)'},
    {r:'r5', name:'Mind Pump Podcast'},
    {r:'r6', name:'Steph Gaudreau  (Harder to Kill)'},
    {r:'r99', name:'None of these'}
  ];
  if(items.length === 0) return;
  var _r99=null;for(var _i=items.length-1;_i&gt;=0;_i--){if(items[_i].r==='r99'){_r99=items.splice(_i,1)[0];break;}}
  for(var _i=items.length-1;_i&gt;0;_i--){var _j=Math.floor(Math.random()*(_i+1));var _t=items[_i];items[_i]=items[_j];items[_j]=_t;}
  if(items.length&gt;25)items.length=25;
  if(_r99)items.push(_r99);
  var checks = {}, noneActive = false, oeNotSure = false;
  var grid = document.getElementById('nm-inf-grid');
  var noneBtn = document.getElementById('nm-inf-none');
  var oeInput = document.getElementById('nm-inf-oe-input');
  var oeNotsure = document.getElementById('nm-inf-oe-notsure');
  var continueBtn = document.getElementById('nm-continue');
  if(grid){
    var ch = '';
    for(var i=0;i&lt;items.length;i++) ch += '&lt;div class="nm-inf-chip" data-row="'+items[i].r+'"&gt;'+items[i].name+'&lt;/div&gt;';
    grid.innerHTML = ch;
    grid.querySelectorAll('.nm-inf-chip').forEach(function(chip){
      chip.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var r = chip.getAttribute('data-row');
        checks[r] = !checks[r];
        chip.classList.toggle('nm-sel', checks[r]);
        nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, r, checks[r]);
        if(checks[r] &amp;&amp; noneActive){
          noneActive = false;
          noneBtn.classList.remove('nm-sel');
          nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, 'r99', false);
        }
      });
    });
  }
  if(noneBtn){
    noneBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      noneActive = !noneActive;
      noneBtn.classList.toggle('nm-sel', noneActive);
      nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, 'r99', noneActive);
      if(noneActive){
        Object.keys(checks).forEach(function(r){ checks[r] = false; });
        grid.querySelectorAll('.nm-inf-chip').forEach(function(c){ c.classList.remove('nm-sel'); });
        var q = nmFindQ(qLabel);
        if(q) q.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(function(cb){
          if(cb.name &amp;&amp; cb.name.indexOf('r99') === -1 &amp;&amp; cb.checked){ cb.click(); }
        });
      }
    });
  }
  if(oeInput){
    oeInput.addEventListener('input', function(){
      nmSyncText(oeLabel, oeInput.value);
      if(oeInput.value.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; oeNotSure){ oeNotSure = false; oeNotsure.classList.remove('nm-sel'); }
    });
  }
  if(oeNotsure){
    oeNotsure.addEventListener('click', function(){
      oeNotSure = !oeNotSure;
      oeNotsure.classList.toggle('nm-sel', oeNotSure);
      if(oeNotSure){ oeInput.value = 'Not Sure'; nmSyncText(oeLabel, 'Not Sure'); }
      else { oeInput.value = ''; nmSyncText(oeLabel, ''); }
    });
  }
  continueBtn.disabled = false;
  if(continueBtn){
    continueBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(continueBtn.disabled) return;
      var anyChecked = Object.keys(checks).some(function(k){ return checks[k]; });
      if(!anyChecked &amp;&amp; !noneActive) nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, 'r99', true);
      nmClickNext();
    });
  }
})();

function nmFindQ(q){
    var el = document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]');
    if(el &amp;&amp; el.closest &amp;&amp; !el.classList.contains('question')){
      var par = el.closest('.question');
      if(par) el = par;
    }
    return el;
}
function nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, rowLabel, checked){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 0: cached lookup */
    if(window._nmCBCache &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel] &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel]){
      inp = window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel];
      if(inp){ if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click(); return; }
      inp = null;
    }
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][value="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name*="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.0.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      var prefix = '';
      for(var pi=0; pi&lt;allCB.length; pi++){
        var nm = allCB[pi].name || '';
        var ld = nm.lastIndexOf('.');
        if(ld &gt; 0){ prefix = nm.substring(0, ld+1); break; }
      }
      if(prefix){
        var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m){
          var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
          if(rNum === 99){
            var maxSfx = -1;
            for(var si=0; si&lt;allCB.length; si++){
              var sfx = parseInt((allCB[si].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
              if(sfx &gt; maxSfx) maxSfx = sfx;
            }
            if(maxSfx &gt;= 0) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+maxSfx+'"]');
          } else {
            inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+(rNum-1)+'"]');
          }
        }
      }
      /* Fallback: position-based (works when no shuffle) */
      if(!inp &amp;&amp; allCB.length &gt; 0){
        var m2 = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m2){
          var idx = parseInt(m2[1], 10);
          if(idx === 99){
            for(var ki=0; ki&lt;allCB.length; ki++){
              var nm2 = (allCB[ki].name||'')+(allCB[ki].className||'');
              if(nm2.indexOf('noanswer')!==-1||nm2.indexOf('exclusive')!==-1){inp=allCB[ki]; break;}
            }
            if(!inp) inp = allCB[allCB.length-1];
          } else if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=allCB.length){
            inp = allCB[idx-1];
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Cache and apply */
    if(inp){
      if(!window._nmCBCache) window._nmCBCache = {};
      if(!window._nmCBCache[qLabel]) window._nmCBCache[qLabel] = {};
      window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel] = inp;
      if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' NO INPUT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncRating(qLabel, rowLabel, colVal){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;all.length; i++){
      var name = all[i].name || '';
      var v = all[i].value;
      if(name.indexOf(rowLabel) !== -1 &amp;&amp; (v === colVal || v === 'c'+colVal)){ inp = all[i]; break; }
    }
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(m){
        var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
        var defIdx = (rNum === 99) ? -1 : rNum - 1;
        /* Try selects first */
        var allSel = box.querySelectorAll('select');
        if(allSel.length &gt; 0){
          var selPrefix = '';
          for(var si=0; si&lt;allSel.length; si++){
            var sn = allSel[si].name || '';
            var sld = sn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(sld &gt; 0){ selPrefix = sn.substring(0, sld+1); break; }
          }
          if(selPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxS = -1;
              for(var sk=0; sk&lt;allSel.length; sk++){
                var ss = parseInt((allSel[sk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(ss &gt; maxS) maxS = ss;
              }
              defIdx = maxS;
            }
            var sel = box.querySelector('select[name="'+selPrefix+defIdx+'"]');
            if(sel){
              sel.value = colVal;
              if(!sel.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel.value = 'c'+colVal;
              sel.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
              try{ jQuery(sel).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
              return;
            }
          }
        }
        /* Try radios by definition-index */
        if(!inp &amp;&amp; all.length &gt; 0){
          var rPrefix = '';
          for(var ri=0; ri&lt;all.length; ri++){
            var rn = all[ri].name || '';
            var rld = rn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(rld &gt; 0){ rPrefix = rn.substring(0, rld+1); break; }
          }
          if(rPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxR = -1;
              var rNames = {};
              for(var rk=0; rk&lt;all.length; rk++){
                var rs = parseInt((all[rk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(rs &gt; maxR) maxR = rs;
              }
              defIdx = maxR;
            }
            var targetName = rPrefix + defIdx;
            for(var rj=0; rj&lt;all.length; rj++){
              if(all[rj].name === targetName &amp;&amp; (all[rj].value === colVal || all[rj].value === 'c'+colVal)){
                inp = all[rj]; break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 3: position-based fallback (works when no shuffle) */
    if(!inp){
      var groups = {};
      for(var k=0; k&lt;all.length; k++){
        var n = all[k].name;
        if(!groups[n]) groups[n] = [];
        groups[n].push(all[k]);
      }
      var gKeys = Object.keys(groups);
      var rowMatch = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(rowMatch &amp;&amp; gKeys.length &gt;= parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)){
        var rowGroup = groups[gKeys[parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)-1]];
        var colMatch = colVal.match ? colVal.match(/^(\d+)$/) : null;
        var cIdx = colMatch ? parseInt(colMatch[1],10)-1 : parseInt(colVal,10)-1;
        if(rowGroup &amp;&amp; cIdx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; cIdx &lt; rowGroup.length){
          inp = rowGroup[cIdx];
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 4: select by name pattern */
    if(!inp){
      var sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name="'+qLabel+'_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(!sel2) sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name*="_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(sel2){
        sel2.value = colVal;
        if(!sel2.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel2.value = 'c'+colVal;
        sel2.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
        try{ jQuery(sel2).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
        return;
      }
    }
    if(inp){
      inp.checked = true;
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' '+rowLabel+'='+colVal+' NOT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncText(qLabel, val){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return;
    var inp = q.querySelector('textarea') || q.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
    if(inp){
        inp.value = val;
        try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('change').trigger('input'); }catch(e){}
    }
}
function nmClickNext(){
    var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
    if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
    } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
    }
}
function nmGetRows(qLabel){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return [];
    var rows = [], seen = {};
    var inputs = q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"], input[type="checkbox"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;inputs.length; i++){
        var inp = inputs[i];
        var name = inp.name || '';
        var m = name.match(new RegExp('^'+qLabel+'_(r\\d+)'));
        if(!m) continue;
        var rLabel = m[1];
        if(seen[rLabel] || rLabel === 'r99') continue;
        seen[rLabel] = true;
        var rowEl = inp.closest('.fir-row') || inp.closest('tr') || inp.closest('.row-elements');
        if(!rowEl) rowEl = inp.parentNode;
        var textEl = rowEl ? (rowEl.querySelector('.fir-text') || rowEl.querySelector('.row-text') || rowEl.querySelector('label')) : null;
        var txt = textEl ? textEl.textContent.trim() : rLabel;
        if(txt === rLabel || txt.length &lt; 2){
            var parent = inp.closest('.fir-row');
            if(parent){
                var fc = parent.querySelector('.fir-text-container, .fir-text, td:first-child, .row-label');
                if(fc) txt = fc.textContent.trim();
            }
        }
        rows.push({r: rLabel, name: txt});
    }
    return rows;
}

(function(){
  var qLabel = 'NM_SRC_T9';
  var oeLabel = 'NM_SRC_T9_OE';
  var items = [
    {r:'r1', name:'Peter Attia  (The Drive)'},
    {r:'r2', name:'Bryan Johnson  (Blueprint)'},
    {r:'r3', name:'David Sinclair  (Lifespan)'},
    {r:'r4', name:'Fight Aging'},
    {r:'r5', name:'Lifespan.io'},
    {r:'r6', name:'Longevity.Technology'},
    {r:'r7', name:'Sergey Young  (Longevity Vision)'},
    {r:'r8', name:'Nir Barzilai  (Age Later)'},
    {r:'r9', name:'Elysium Health Insights'},
    {r:'r10', name:'Peter Attia  (Outlive)'},
    {r:'r11', name:'Nir Eyal  (Indistractable Health)'},
    {r:'r12', name:'LifeOmic  (Longevity Science)'}
  ];
  if(items.length === 0) return;
  var _qBox = nmFindQ(qLabel);
  if(_qBox){var _allEls=_qBox.querySelectorAll('input,select');var _names={};_allEls.forEach(function(el){if(el.name)_names[el.name]=true;});var _sfx={};for(var _k in _names){var _p=_k.split('.');var _s=parseInt(_p[_p.length-1],10);if(!isNaN(_s))_sfx[_s]=true;}var _sfxCount=Object.keys(_sfx).length;console.warn('[nmFilter] '+qLabel+' els='+_allEls.length+' sfxCount='+_sfxCount+' before='+items.length);if(_sfxCount&gt;0&amp;&amp;_sfxCount&lt;items.length){items=items.filter(function(it,idx){return _sfx[idx];});console.warn('[nmFilter] '+qLabel+' after='+items.length);}}
  if(items.length === 0){console.warn('[nmFilter] '+qLabel+' EMPTY after filter, skipping'); return;}
  for(var _i=items.length-1;_i&gt;0;_i--){var _j=Math.floor(Math.random()*(_i+1));var _t=items[_i];items[_i]=items[_j];items[_j]=_t;}
  if(items.length&gt;25)items.length=25;
  var swipeIdx = 0, swipeAnswers = {}, oeNotSure = false;
  var cardText = document.getElementById('nm-card-text');
  var freqBtns = document.getElementById('nm-freq-btns');
  var dotsEl = document.getElementById('nm-dots');
  var counterEl = document.getElementById('nm-swipe-counter');
  var oeWrap = document.getElementById('nm-oe-wrap');
  var oeInput = document.getElementById('nm-oe-input');
  var oeNotsure = document.getElementById('nm-oe-notsure');
  var continueBtn = document.getElementById('nm-continue');
  if(dotsEl){
    var dh = '';
    for(var i=0;i&lt;items.length;i++) dh += '&lt;div class="nm-swipe-dot'+(i===0?' nm-active':'')+'" data-idx="'+i+'"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
    dotsEl.innerHTML = dh;
  }
  function updateSwipe(){
    if(!cardText) return;
    cardText.textContent = items[swipeIdx].name;
    if(counterEl) counterEl.textContent = (swipeIdx+1)+' of '+items.length;
    if(freqBtns){
      var cur = swipeAnswers[items[swipeIdx].r];
      freqBtns.querySelectorAll('.nm-freq-btn-v2').forEach(function(b){
        b.classList.remove('nm-flash');
        b.classList.toggle('nm-sel', b.getAttribute('data-col') === cur);
      });
    }
    if(dotsEl){
      dotsEl.querySelectorAll('.nm-swipe-dot').forEach(function(dot, i){
        dot.classList.toggle('nm-active', i === swipeIdx);
        dot.classList.toggle('nm-done', !!swipeAnswers[items[i].r]);
      });
    }
  }
  function updateContinue(){
    var allRated = items.every(function(item){ return swipeAnswers[item.r]; });
    continueBtn.disabled = !allRated;
    if(allRated &amp;&amp; oeWrap) oeWrap.style.display = '';
  }
  if(freqBtns){
    freqBtns.querySelectorAll('.nm-freq-btn-v2').forEach(function(btn){
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var col = btn.getAttribute('data-col');
        var val = btn.getAttribute('data-val');
        swipeAnswers[items[swipeIdx].r] = col;
        nmSyncRating(qLabel, items[swipeIdx].r, val);
        freqBtns.querySelectorAll('.nm-freq-btn-v2').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('nm-sel','nm-flash'); });
        btn.classList.add('nm-flash');
        setTimeout(function(){
          btn.classList.remove('nm-flash');
          btn.classList.add('nm-sel');
          if(swipeIdx &lt; items.length - 1){
            setTimeout(function(){ swipeIdx++; updateSwipe(); }, 150);
          } else {
            updateSwipe();
          }
          updateContinue();
        }, 400);
      });
    });
  }
  if(oeInput){
    oeInput.addEventListener('input', function(){
      nmSyncText(oeLabel, oeInput.value);
      if(oeInput.value.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; oeNotSure){ oeNotSure = false; oeNotsure.classList.remove('nm-sel'); }
    });
  }
  if(oeNotsure){
    oeNotsure.addEventListener('click', function(){
      oeNotSure = !oeNotSure;
      oeNotsure.classList.toggle('nm-sel', oeNotSure);
      if(oeNotSure){ oeInput.value = 'Not Sure'; nmSyncText(oeLabel, 'Not Sure'); }
      else { oeInput.value = ''; nmSyncText(oeLabel, ''); }
    });
  }
  if(dotsEl){
    dotsEl.querySelectorAll('.nm-swipe-dot').forEach(function(dot){
      dot.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var idx = parseInt(dot.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
        if(!isNaN(idx) &amp;&amp; idx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; idx &lt; items.length){ swipeIdx = idx; updateSwipe(); }
      });
    });
  }
  if(continueBtn){
    continueBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(continueBtn.disabled) return;
      nmClickNext();
    });
  }
  updateSwipe();
  updateContinue();
})();

  &lt;div class="nm-continue-wrap"&gt;
    &lt;div class="nm-error-prompt" id="nm-error"&gt;Please answer before continuing.&lt;/div&gt;

function nmFindQ(q){
    var el = document.getElementById('q_'+q)
        || document.getElementById('question_'+q)
        || document.getElementById(q)
        || document.querySelector('[id$="_'+q+'"]');
    if(el &amp;&amp; el.closest &amp;&amp; !el.classList.contains('question')){
      var par = el.closest('.question');
      if(par) el = par;
    }
    return el;
}
function nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, rowLabel, checked){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 0: cached lookup */
    if(window._nmCBCache &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel] &amp;&amp; window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel]){
      inp = window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel];
      if(inp){ if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click(); return; }
      inp = null;
    }
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][value="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    if(!inp) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name*="'+rowLabel+'"]');
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.0.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var allCB = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      var prefix = '';
      for(var pi=0; pi&lt;allCB.length; pi++){
        var nm = allCB[pi].name || '';
        var ld = nm.lastIndexOf('.');
        if(ld &gt; 0){ prefix = nm.substring(0, ld+1); break; }
      }
      if(prefix){
        var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m){
          var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
          if(rNum === 99){
            var maxSfx = -1;
            for(var si=0; si&lt;allCB.length; si++){
              var sfx = parseInt((allCB[si].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
              if(sfx &gt; maxSfx) maxSfx = sfx;
            }
            if(maxSfx &gt;= 0) inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+maxSfx+'"]');
          } else {
            inp = box.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"][name="'+prefix+(rNum-1)+'"]');
          }
        }
      }
      /* Fallback: position-based (works when no shuffle) */
      if(!inp &amp;&amp; allCB.length &gt; 0){
        var m2 = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
        if(m2){
          var idx = parseInt(m2[1], 10);
          if(idx === 99){
            for(var ki=0; ki&lt;allCB.length; ki++){
              var nm2 = (allCB[ki].name||'')+(allCB[ki].className||'');
              if(nm2.indexOf('noanswer')!==-1||nm2.indexOf('exclusive')!==-1){inp=allCB[ki]; break;}
            }
            if(!inp) inp = allCB[allCB.length-1];
          } else if(idx&gt;0 &amp;&amp; idx&lt;=allCB.length){
            inp = allCB[idx-1];
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Cache and apply */
    if(inp){
      if(!window._nmCBCache) window._nmCBCache = {};
      if(!window._nmCBCache[qLabel]) window._nmCBCache[qLabel] = {};
      window._nmCBCache[qLabel][rowLabel] = inp;
      if(inp.checked !== checked) inp.click();
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncCB] '+qLabel+'.'+rowLabel+' NO INPUT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncRating(qLabel, rowLabel, colVal){
    var box = nmFindQ(qLabel);
    if(!box){ console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' NOT FOUND'); return; }
    var inp = null;
    /* Strategy 1: standard Decipher name patterns */
    var all = box.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;all.length; i++){
      var name = all[i].name || '';
      var v = all[i].value;
      if(name.indexOf(rowLabel) !== -1 &amp;&amp; (v === colVal || v === 'c'+colVal)){ inp = all[i]; break; }
    }
    /* Strategy 2: definition-index via ans{id}.{idx} naming */
    if(!inp){
      var m = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(m){
        var rNum = parseInt(m[1], 10);
        var defIdx = (rNum === 99) ? -1 : rNum - 1;
        /* Try selects first */
        var allSel = box.querySelectorAll('select');
        if(allSel.length &gt; 0){
          var selPrefix = '';
          for(var si=0; si&lt;allSel.length; si++){
            var sn = allSel[si].name || '';
            var sld = sn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(sld &gt; 0){ selPrefix = sn.substring(0, sld+1); break; }
          }
          if(selPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxS = -1;
              for(var sk=0; sk&lt;allSel.length; sk++){
                var ss = parseInt((allSel[sk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(ss &gt; maxS) maxS = ss;
              }
              defIdx = maxS;
            }
            var sel = box.querySelector('select[name="'+selPrefix+defIdx+'"]');
            if(sel){
              sel.value = colVal;
              if(!sel.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel.value = 'c'+colVal;
              sel.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
              try{ jQuery(sel).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
              return;
            }
          }
        }
        /* Try radios by definition-index */
        if(!inp &amp;&amp; all.length &gt; 0){
          var rPrefix = '';
          for(var ri=0; ri&lt;all.length; ri++){
            var rn = all[ri].name || '';
            var rld = rn.lastIndexOf('.');
            if(rld &gt; 0){ rPrefix = rn.substring(0, rld+1); break; }
          }
          if(rPrefix){
            if(rNum === 99){
              var maxR = -1;
              var rNames = {};
              for(var rk=0; rk&lt;all.length; rk++){
                var rs = parseInt((all[rk].name||'').split('.').pop(), 10);
                if(rs &gt; maxR) maxR = rs;
              }
              defIdx = maxR;
            }
            var targetName = rPrefix + defIdx;
            for(var rj=0; rj&lt;all.length; rj++){
              if(all[rj].name === targetName &amp;&amp; (all[rj].value === colVal || all[rj].value === 'c'+colVal)){
                inp = all[rj]; break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 3: position-based fallback (works when no shuffle) */
    if(!inp){
      var groups = {};
      for(var k=0; k&lt;all.length; k++){
        var n = all[k].name;
        if(!groups[n]) groups[n] = [];
        groups[n].push(all[k]);
      }
      var gKeys = Object.keys(groups);
      var rowMatch = rowLabel.match(/^r(\d+)$/);
      if(rowMatch &amp;&amp; gKeys.length &gt;= parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)){
        var rowGroup = groups[gKeys[parseInt(rowMatch[1],10)-1]];
        var colMatch = colVal.match ? colVal.match(/^(\d+)$/) : null;
        var cIdx = colMatch ? parseInt(colMatch[1],10)-1 : parseInt(colVal,10)-1;
        if(rowGroup &amp;&amp; cIdx &gt;= 0 &amp;&amp; cIdx &lt; rowGroup.length){
          inp = rowGroup[cIdx];
        }
      }
    }
    /* Strategy 4: select by name pattern */
    if(!inp){
      var sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name="'+qLabel+'_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(!sel2) sel2 = box.querySelector('select[name*="_'+rowLabel+'"]');
      if(sel2){
        sel2.value = colVal;
        if(!sel2.querySelector('option[value="'+colVal+'"]')) sel2.value = 'c'+colVal;
        sel2.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
        try{ jQuery(sel2).trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
        return;
      }
    }
    if(inp){
      inp.checked = true;
      inp.click();
      inp.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true}));
      try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('click').trigger('change'); }catch(e){}
    } else {
      console.warn('[nmSyncRating] '+qLabel+' '+rowLabel+'='+colVal+' NOT FOUND');
    }
}
function nmSyncText(qLabel, val){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return;
    var inp = q.querySelector('textarea') || q.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
    if(inp){
        inp.value = val;
        try{ jQuery(inp).trigger('change').trigger('input'); }catch(e){}
    }
}
function nmClickNext(){
    var nxt = document.querySelector('.nextPage, .button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if(!nxt) nxt = document.querySelector('.button, input.button');
    if(nxt){
        nxt.setAttribute('style','display:block !important;visibility:hidden;position:absolute;left:-9999px;');
        nxt.click();
    } else {
        var form = document.querySelector('form');
        if(form) form.submit();
    }
}
function nmGetRows(qLabel){
    var q = nmFindQ(qLabel); if(!q) return [];
    var rows = [], seen = {};
    var inputs = q.querySelectorAll('input[type="radio"], input[type="checkbox"]');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;inputs.length; i++){
        var inp = inputs[i];
        var name = inp.name || '';
        var m = name.match(new RegExp('^'+qLabel+'_(r\\d+)'));
        if(!m) continue;
        var rLabel = m[1];
        if(seen[rLabel] || rLabel === 'r99') continue;
        seen[rLabel] = true;
        var rowEl = inp.closest('.fir-row') || inp.closest('tr') || inp.closest('.row-elements');
        if(!rowEl) rowEl = inp.parentNode;
        var textEl = rowEl ? (rowEl.querySelector('.fir-text') || rowEl.querySelector('.row-text') || rowEl.querySelector('label')) : null;
        var txt = textEl ? textEl.textContent.trim() : rLabel;
        if(txt === rLabel || txt.length &lt; 2){
            var parent = inp.closest('.fir-row');
            if(parent){
                var fc = parent.querySelector('.fir-text-container, .fir-text, td:first-child, .row-label');
                if(fc) txt = fc.textContent.trim();
            }
        }
        rows.push({r: rLabel, name: txt});
    }
    return rows;
}

(function(){
  var qLabel = 'NM_INF_T9';
  var oeLabel = 'NM_INF_T9_OE';
  var items = [
    {r:'r1', name:'Peter Attia  (The Drive)'},
    {r:'r2', name:'Bryan Johnson  (Blueprint)'},

    {r:'r6', name:'Casey Means'},
    {r:'r99', name:'None of these'}
  ];
  if(items.length === 0) return;
  var _r99=null;for(var _i=items.length-1;_i&gt;=0;_i--){if(items[_i].r==='r99'){_r99=items.splice(_i,1)[0];break;}}
  for(var _i=items.length-1;_i&gt;0;_i--){var _j=Math.floor(Math.random()*(_i+1));var _t=items[_i];items[_i]=items[_j];items[_j]=_t;}
  if(items.length&gt;25)items.length=25;
  if(_r99)items.push(_r99);
  var checks = {}, noneActive = false, oeNotSure = false;
  var grid = document.getElementById('nm-inf-grid');
  var noneBtn = document.getElementById('nm-inf-none');
  var oeInput = document.getElementById('nm-inf-oe-input');
  var oeNotsure = document.getElementById('nm-inf-oe-notsure');
  var continueBtn = document.getElementById('nm-continue');
  if(grid){
    var ch = '';
    for(var i=0;i&lt;items.length;i++) ch += '&lt;div class="nm-inf-chip" data-row="'+items[i].r+'"&gt;'+items[i].name+'&lt;/div&gt;';
    grid.innerHTML = ch;
    grid.querySelectorAll('.nm-inf-chip').forEach(function(chip){
      chip.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var r = chip.getAttribute('data-row');
        checks[r] = !checks[r];
        chip.classList.toggle('nm-sel', checks[r]);
        nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, r, checks[r]);
        if(checks[r] &amp;&amp; noneActive){
          noneActive = false;
          noneBtn.classList.remove('nm-sel');
          nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, 'r99', false);
        }
      });
    });
  }
  if(noneBtn){
    noneBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      noneActive = !noneActive;
      noneBtn.classList.toggle('nm-sel', noneActive);
      nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, 'r99', noneActive);
      if(noneActive){
        Object.keys(checks).forEach(function(r){ checks[r] = false; });
        grid.querySelectorAll('.nm-inf-chip').forEach(function(c){ c.classList.remove('nm-sel'); });
        var q = nmFindQ(qLabel);
        if(q) q.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(function(cb){
          if(cb.name &amp;&amp; cb.name.indexOf('r99') === -1 &amp;&amp; cb.checked){ cb.click(); }
        });
      }
    });
  }
  if(oeInput){
    oeInput.addEventListener('input', function(){
      nmSyncText(oeLabel, oeInput.value);
      if(oeInput.value.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; oeNotSure){ oeNotSure = false; oeNotsure.classList.remove('nm-sel'); }
    });
  }
  if(oeNotsure){
    oeNotsure.addEventListener('click', function(){
      oeNotSure = !oeNotSure;
      oeNotsure.classList.toggle('nm-sel', oeNotSure);
      if(oeNotSure){ oeInput.value = 'Not Sure'; nmSyncText(oeLabel, 'Not Sure'); }
      else { oeInput.value = ''; nmSyncText(oeLabel, ''); }
    });
  }
  continueBtn.disabled = false;
  if(continueBtn){
    continueBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(continueBtn.disabled) return;
      var anyChecked = Object.keys(checks).some(function(k){ return checks[k]; });
      if(!anyChecked &amp;&amp; !noneActive) nmSyncCheckbox(qLabel, 'r99', true);
      nmClickNext();
    });
  }
})();
